In the morning, 700 rickshaw pullers gathered at the station and were persuaded to disperse by the military police. Then they formed groups, holding bricks and stones, and destroyed联运and operating cars. Local military police were dispatched in full force and spread throughout the streets to maintain law and order. The Public Security Bureau ordered all street cleaners to pull rickshaws, but it was of no avail. The Security Office convened a meeting of all circles on the 27th, but it was dismissed without results because the capitalists refused to make concessions. Various agencies are scheduled to hold another meeting on the 28th, and decisive measures will be taken, which may be resolved. The Garrison Command announced martial law in the evening. (Special telegram on the 27th)

Opinions of the Ministry of Interior on Unifying Water Conservancy Agencies

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior drafted opinions on unifying water conservancy agencies and submitted them to the Executive Yuan. The Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee passed the principles and handed them over to the Central Political Conference for review. The content of the case is that the current recurring expenses of various water conservancy agencies across the country are about 300,000 yuan per month according to the national budget, but the actual expenditure is more than 100,000 yuan. If they are unified and merged to establish a central water conservancy agency, either the Ministry of Water Conservancy or the Central Water Conservancy Commission, engineering offices can be established in various places according to actual needs, surveying teams can be organized, and a portion of the total recurring expenses can be saved for engineering projects. All water conservancy economic plans can also be uniformly submitted to the National Economic Commission for design, which will be more effective with less effort. After a decision is made, it will be promulgated by the National Government. (Special telegram on the 27th)

German-Polish Non-Aggression Pact Concluded 45

Ten Years of Peace Guaranteed

Mixed Reactions from Various Countries Upon Hearing the News

(Berlin) The ten-year non-aggression treaty between Germany and Poland, based on the Kellogg-Briand Pact, has been concluded today. In the future, any disputes between the two countries will be resolved without resorting to force. (Reuters telegram on the 26th)

Paris Informed sources here do not find the conclusion of a non-aggression treaty between Poland and Germany surprising. They say it is the result of a meeting between German Chancellor Hitler and Polish Ambassador to Germany Lipski on January 15. It is generally believed that Poland and France are allied and friendly countries, and that improving relations with Germany will effectively promote peace, thereby obtaining new security guarantees to consolidate its position. (Havas telegram on the 26th)

Prague The Czech government was surprised to learn of the news of German-Polish cooperation. However, the Czech newspapers did not have time to comment on the news, so there is no expression yet. (Guomin telegram on the 27th)

(London) The newspapers here greatly approve of the union of Germany and Poland, because this move can show Germany's intention to be peaceful to the utmost. Even the Daily Leader, which has always opposed the German National Socialist Party, said that this German-Polish union can resolve the discord between European countries. Although France is slightly hit, it can also reduce many obstacles in the future. The Daily Mail also said that Hitler and Piłsudski signed this treaty to put Europe on the right track. The London Times correspondent in Germany said in a dispatch that the conclusion of a sincere and friendly treaty between the two countries is indeed an innovation. Although Germans still dare not believe that there will be no other deterioration in the future, in reality, Germany and Poland will become more harmonious as a result. (Guomin telegram on the 27th)

(Berlin) The people here are ecstatic about the signing of the ten-year non-aggression treaty between Germany and Poland. Paris, London, and Warsaw are also deeply pleased, because the impact of this treaty is not limited to the two countries, and the world situation can also benefit from it. All circles in Berlin believe that this treaty is a success of Hitler's new policy, so it can be used to express Germany's repeatedly expressed sincerity to be peaceful and to have mutual understanding between countries. The Berlin Daily News and others commented that this treaty does not hinder other countries, nor does it have any intention against France or Russia. It is specifically aimed at making diplomatic relations last forever. (Guomin telegram on the 27th)

Britain Drafts Declaration to Mediate the Franco-German Stalemate 46

To Be Read to Parliament Tomorrow

(London) When Parliament reconvenes on January 29, British Foreign Secretary Simon will announce Britain's new policy on disarmament. This declaration may be based on the British disarmament draft, as the British government has never had any major deviations from it. However, it is expected that the government will revise it in light of recent events. Today, Prime Minister MacDonald, Foreign Secretary Simon, Secretary of War Hailsham, Secretary of the Navy Monsell, Dominions Secretary Thomas, and Lord Privy Seal Eden considered the final draft of the declaration in the Disarmament Subcommittee. The disarmament issue was studied very thoroughly at that time, as it is expected that when Parliament reconvenes, members of all parties will raise various questions about the government's policy. At the same time, all parties are also demanding that the government take action. Berlin has asked Britain to put forward new proposals to mediate and break the stalemate between France and Germany. Members of all parties in the country also advocate that the government should abandon its policy of quiet observation and offer advice on European affairs. Judging from the situation, Britain may advise France not to make the trial period a condition for any concessions to Germany. However, France's concessions may be subject to a requirement that Britain assume a new and practical obligation to prevent anyone from violating the disarmament convention that may be agreed upon in the future. However, the British public will strongly oppose this additional obligation. Another possibility is that Britain may propose that the various weapons of a defensive nature that are permitted be reclassified as prohibited weapons of an aggressive nature, to prevent Germany from having too strong military strength in the future when Germany is allowed military equality. (Reuters telegram on the 26th)

Balkan Non-Aggression Pact 47

Can Be Signed on February 2

Seanyaj Romania's King Carol hosted Bulgaria's King Boris in this city. Rome Foreign Minister Titulescu's ear disease has not healed, so he cannot attend the meeting between the Romanian King and the Bulgarian King in Seanyaj. Yugoslavia, and other countries. As for Bulgaria, it is free to add this pact within a certain period of time in the future. It is reported that the future non-aggression pact in the Balkans stipulates that the contracting countries guarantee each other's territorial integrity and secondly, guarantee the security of each other's borders.

The reason why Bulgaria opposes the new pact is related to these treaties. The Bulgarian government is originally dissatisfied with the borders set by the peace treaty. The newly signed Balkan non-aggression treaty is like adding another layer of protection to the peace treaty, so Bulgaria cannot agree to it. (Havas telegram on the 27th)

All Europeans are Paying Attention to the Conflict Between Hitler and Goering Incompatibility of Views on Restoration and Austria Great Impact of Two Strongmen Not Coexisting 48

(London) German Chancellor Hitler and Prussian Prime Minister Goering are both the most determined people in modern Europe. The world regards Goering as Hitler's right-hand man, but recently the three have had disagreements and repeated quarrels. This is the latest scene in the National Socialist Party, and all Europeans are paying attention to the outcome.

It is still difficult to predict.

The points of disagreement between the two are as follows: (1) Germany wants to make Austria a National Socialist state, and must first remove Austrian Chancellor Dollfuss. Hitler recently saw the great powers expressing sympathy for Austria and wanted to slightly change his policy towards the Austrian Chancellor, but Goering strongly opposed it, putting Hitler in a dilemma. (2) Goering seems to want to restore the royal family and give them back political power, but Hitler does not want to abolish the throne and restore it, and to reduce his own authority, so he opposes restoration with all his might. (3) Dimitarov, a Bulgarian Communist,

was previously suspected of arson in the Reichstag, and although he has been acquitted, he is still imprisoned. Hitler wanted to release him,

even though Dimitrov may make powerful propaganda against the National Socialist Party in other countries, it is impossible to prevent this and imprison him forever, but Goering does not advocate this. (4) Hitler's proposed new German constitution wants to reduce the land of Prussia, which is also something that Goering cannot agree to. (5) On the issue of religious disputes, Hitler advocated that Müller, the head of the Protestant Church of Germany, should take a leave of absence and temporarily have others handle religious improvement matters to avoid political forces, but Goering replied, "When we put on brown shirts, we are neither Christians nor Catholics." Goering advocated that religion should obey the state, so the reconciliation of religious disputes has been difficult to achieve.

All five of these points are the reasons why Hitler and Goering are gradually becoming incompatible. Although the majority of the German people support Hitler, Goering is not without followers. If the conflict between the two intensifies, there will be very important developments in Germany. (Reuters telegram on the 27th)

(Berlin) Last night, when the National Military Officers' Association was celebrating the 75th birthday of the deposed emperor, suddenly heavy trucks carrying police and stormtroopers sped to the scene, surrounding the venue. According to the old custom, all the officers had to stand up to raise a glass to bless the deposed emperor at the sound of the twelve o'clock bell. At this time, the police rushed in, ordered everyone to raise their hands, and ordered the officers in imperial military uniforms to go home immediately. The celebration was not held. In previous years, this celebration was not restricted. (Reuters telegram on the 27th)

American Business Revival 51

Both Imports and Exports Showed an Increase

(Washington) According to figures released today, American exports and imports both increased in 1933. Imports for the year totaled $1,449,000,000, an increase of $126,000,000 over 1932. Exports totaled $1,675,000,000, an increase of $64,000,000 over 1932. Exports for December were valued at $192,000,000, an increase of $8,000,000 over November. Imports totaled $133,000,000,

also an increase of $5,000,000. (Reuter, 26th)

(Washington) The Senate today took decisive action on the President's monetary bill, authorizing the Secretary of the Treasury, by a vote of 54 to 36, to manage the equalization fund independently, rejecting an amendment to organize a five-member committee of the Banking Committee to manage the fund, and passing an amendment to limit the period of operation of the equalization fund and the President's power to reduce the value of the dollar to two years, but extendable to three years. During today's debate, Democratic Senator Pittman advocated expanding the President's powers to issue silver certificates in exchange for silver bullion for use in place of silver dollars. Republican Reed denounced the potential impact of the monetary bill, saying the equalization fund would create an artificial market for government bonds and keep bond prices at a fixed level. Democrat Robinson said Reed's proposal was merely a continuation of former President Hoover's "laissez-faire" policy. Democrat Bailey said the bill was aimed at protecting the United States from currency wars with countries with depreciated currencies and reducing the burden of debt on the American people. Senator Borah advocated restoring silver coinage to expand the world's monetary standard, saying gold was scarce and unevenly distributed, and the monetary bill would allocate gold to address this problem, but would not benefit the rest of the world. (Reuter, 26th)

1935 Naval Conference: Japan Will Demand Changes to Ratios; Navy Minister Osumi Declares to the House 52

Army Minister Hayashi Says Japan and Russia are Both Adopting Defensive Armaments

(Tokyo) At the general budget meeting of the House of Representatives on the 27th, Seiyukai member Shinya Uchida raised questions regarding arms reduction, saying that the Japanese arms reduction proposal submitted to the Geneva Disarmament Conference the year before last December stated, "This arms reduction proposal is a suitable case to replace both the Washington and London Treaties." In the future, when the disarmament conference is held in 1935, Japan will inevitably be bound by it, so why does the government not withdraw this proposal? Navy Minister Osumi

replied to this, saying that this proposal has not been included in the discussion topics of the disarmament conference, and there has been no opportunity to clarify the content. Various countries have repeatedly put forward proposals and changed their content each time, so Japan can also follow their example and change the content. We, as the Navy Minister, have just realized the government's opinion that Japan will not be bound by Japan's previous proposal at the 1935 disarmament conference and intends to submit a new arms reduction proposal demanding changes to the ratios. (Jiji News Agency, 27th)

(Tokyo) The House of Representatives opened the general budget meeting at 10:00 this morning. Seiyukai member Shinya Uchida continued to question the naval issue because yesterday's questioning was incomplete. Uchida asked, "I think the crisis of 1935 is due to the result of the London Treaty. How will the government change?"

Navy Minister Osumi replied, "The direct cause does not seem to be the result of the London Treaty, but it can be said to be one of the causes of the crisis." Uchida then advanced his argument, discussing the impropriety of implementing tax cuts based on the London Treaty and the attitude of the army during the major reorganization at the time, saying, "As a result of the establishment of the London Treaty, the government reluctantly implemented a tax cut of 13 million yen, and therefore today it has to implement a 120 million yen naval replenishment plan to compensate for the defects of the treaty. According to the verdict of the May 15th Incident, the young officers said that the defects of the London Treaty should be the responsibility of the political parties. May I ask whether the Navy Minister admits that the responsibility lies with the political parties?"

Navy Minister Osumi replied, "The political parties have no responsibility, and it would have been better if the tax cuts had not been implemented."

At this time, members of the Minseito party loudly criticized the Navy Minister's statement that tax cuts were not good. Navy Minister Osumi continued, saying that the tax cuts were implemented before he took office as Navy Minister, so he withdrew his opinion on this issue. The naval authorities only have one way to clear the past and do their best for the future.

After the Navy Minister's reply, Uchida's argument became more specialized, and he questioned what the ratio of naval power between Japan and the United States would be after the completion of the second replenishment plan, and mentioned the Washington and London Treaties, saying, "According to American newspapers, the Navy Minister's opinion is that Japan is dissatisfied with the ratio of the naval treaties and therefore demands revision. Does the Navy Minister admit this?"

Navy Minister Osumi replied, "I admit it."

Uchida asked, "Since you are dissatisfied with the ratio issue,

what is the Navy Department's policy on issuing a notice of termination of the two treaties within this year?"

Navy Minister Osumi replied, "After investigating all parties and the situation within this year, we will decide on a policy."

Uchida's questioning ended here. Then, Minseito member Masatoshi Takagi questioned the Foreign Minister and asked what the Foreign Minister's opinion was on the ratio issue.

Foreign Minister Hirota replied, "The issue of maintaining the average national defense with the ratio issue has only been experienced for a dozen years since the beginning of mankind. It cannot be said whether the issue of ratio limits is appropriate or not." Takagi did not change his line of attack and pressed the Foreign Minister, saying, "Then does the Foreign Minister have any intention of demanding a change in the ratio?"

Foreign Minister Hirota replied, "My reply to this is the same as Navy Minister Osumi's

reply."

Navy Minister Osumi also stood up and replied, "The naval authorities intend to demand a revision of the ratio." Thereupon, members of both the Seiyu and Minsei parties requested that reference materials be submitted. The chairman adjourned the meeting at 11:30.

The budget meeting reopened at 1:16 p.m. Seiyukai member Shigemasa Sunada was the questioner. Sunada focused his questioning on rural issues, raising issues such as the current situation relief projects and the rural issues of the cabinet meetings. Then, he spoke about the economic conditions of farm households, saying, "According to statistics from the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, the expenditure of rural villages exceeded income by 129 million yen in 1932 and 85.7 million yen in 1933. Although the government has reduced taxes, I am afraid it cannot compensate for such a huge number. The fundamental solution is only to raise the price of agricultural products. What is the government's view?"

Agriculture Minister Goto replied, "The government is considering the issue of raising the price of agricultural products."

Sunada said, "The rice control law does not have the effect of raising the price of rice."

Agriculture Minister Goto replied, "Since the government implemented the rice control law, the price of rice has been stabilized."

Sunada then criticized the government for not having a fundamental policy to deal with excessive rice production and mentioned issues such as silk and raw silk, and warned the government to establish a fundamental policy for sericulture as soon as possible. Then, he questioned the financial authorities, "What kind of response does the government have to the international situation of forming an economic alliance?"

After several debates with Finance Minister Takahashi, Sunada stopped questioning. Next to take the stand to question was Minseito member Katsu Kawasaki. Kawasaki questioned the newly appointed Army Minister, Korekiyo Hayashi, about the reason for reducing the Manchurian Incident expenses and said, "From which year will the name of the Manchurian Incident expenses be abolished as special expenses and made ordinary expenses?"

Army Minister Hayashi replied, "The suppression of bandits in 'Manchukuo' is no longer as intense as before, and the use of bullets has been greatly reduced, so the incident expenses have been reduced. I cannot say from which year the abolishment of special expenses will be abolished."

Kawasaki asked, "Which country will bear the national defense expenses of Manchukuo in the future, Japan or Manchukuo?"

Director of the Deep Reason Bureau, Onodera, replied, "It is not convenient to say this."

Kawasaki then questioned the issue of the security burden of the Manchurian railways, the security improvement expenses after next year, and the relationship between Japan and Russia on the Russo-Manchurian border, etc.

The Army Minister replied, "Although there are various rumors, there is no reason for an incident to occur between Japan and Russia. Japan adopts defensive armaments, and so does Soviet Russia."

Kawasaki then turned his questioning to Home Minister Yamamoto and Finance Minister Takahashi, raising the issue of the current situation relief expenses and financial issues, saying, "If Japanese finance is promoted with today's policy, I am afraid of its future. The Finance Minister intends to establish a financial plan with natural revenue increase as the source of funds. Will this not destabilize finance?" Finance Minister Takahashi replied, "I do not intend to reform finance with natural revenue increase as the source of funds. I said that when there is a time of natural revenue increase, there will be an opportunity to establish tax increases or other reforms." At 6:00 p.m., the Speaker announced the adjournment. (Jiji News Agency, 27th)

Russian Newspaper Comments on Japanese Political Situation 53

Insufficient to Prove Change in Japanese Policy

(Moscow) The newspaper Pravda commented on the speech of Japanese Foreign Minister Koki Hirota, saying that Hirota obviously wanted to evade the responsibility of the Japanese government's forcing Soviet-Japanese relations to become tense by saying that the Soviet Union's position had changed, and at the same time wanted to place this responsibility on the shoulders of the Soviet government with peaceful rhetoric. The Soviet Union's peaceful policy has not changed in the slightest. What should be regretted is that Hirota's speech and General Hayashi's succession to Araki as Army Minister have not shown any change in the Japanese government's foreign policy that can truly maintain peace. If Japan wants to maintain the steps taken by the Soviet government and try to eliminate the insecure diplomatic relations between the Soviet Union and Japan, then its government's foreign policy must have this kind of change, that is, it must not allow the plan to invade the Soviet Union to be realized, and this plan is being planned by the Japanese military and others who support anti-Soviet aggressive adventures. Mussolini Leads Anti-Japanese Front 54

Japanese Ambassador Raises Questions

Rome Dispatch The Japanese Ambassador to Italy, Matsushima, met with Prime Minister Mussolini yesterday and said that he was instructed by the Japanese government to ask Mussolini to explain the political significance of his article "Far East". The article was written by Mussolini for the American news agency and was published in the "Italian People's Daily" on January 7. According to the Japanese side, Mussolini's arguments about Japan in the article seemed unreasonable. The gist of the article was that after Japan withdrew from the League of Nations, it could do whatever it wanted in terms of peace or war, and that there was indeed a danger of war at present. Therefore, since the article was written by the Italian Prime Minister, it had a great impact, and Italian newspapers expressed more opinions based on this, taking the same tone as the Italian Prime Minister, and even Italian official documents often revealed this view, such as the naval budget report submitted by the Senate, which had a similar tone. However, Ambassador Matsushima did not mention this kind of document related to Italian internal affairs when he met with Mussolini, only saying that the economic relations between Italy and Japan were quite good, and there was no political dispute between the two countries. Italy has less relationship with the Far Eastern issue than other European countries, but now it wants to occupy the leading position in the European anti-Japanese imperialism movement. What is the reason? Italian newspapers deliberately used the dangerous rhetoric of "Yellow Peril" to sensationalize and arouse the spirit of cooperation among European countries. The Japanese ambassador specifically questioned the Italian Prime Minister on this point. (Havas, 27th)

India Raises Tariffs to Exclude Japanese Rayon 55

Japan Greatly Alarmed Again

New Delhi It seems that the Indian government has recently raised import duties on rayon. On the 26th, the Commissioner of Commerce, Bhore, notified the Japanese representative, Sawada, that he intends to submit a bill to the Central Legislative Assembly in early February to raise rayon tariffs to protect the Indian domestic cotton industry, but it is not yet clear what the amount of the increase will be. (Jiji News Agency, 26th)

New Delhi The Japanese market was shaken by rumors that India would raise import duties on rayon. Representative Sawada visited the Indian Commissioner of Commerce, Bhore, on the 26th to inquire about this matter. After Bhore acknowledged this fact, he expressed the Indian government's opinion that the Indian cotton industry has recently been oppressed by rayon, and he intends to submit an import tariff bill for rayon products to the Central Legislative Assembly on February 5. After receiving this definite answer, the Japanese delegation suddenly expressed a tense atmosphere. The director of the Trade Bureau, Terao, postponed his departure for New Delhi. India suddenly raised tariffs on groceries last time, and now it has done this again. The Japanese delegation believes that India is not sincere, so it has decided to immediately consult with the domestic government on countermeasures. (Jiji News Agency, 26th)

Kobe According to a telegram received by local traders, when the issue of raising tariffs on groceries became a problem, the Indian parliament further increased the import of silk fabrics for the purpose of increasing tariffs by 50% to 60%, a high rate that can be prohibited, which is extremely noteworthy. The industry immediately informed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of this matter, and it was heard that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs also received a telegram, but the additional tax of 50% to 60% plus the current rate reached a high rate of 100% to 110%. Japan's exports of silk fabrics to India can only be completely wiped out. Soviet Russian Communist Party Congress Stalin Deeply Supported by the Masses Molotov Speaks on Socialism (Moscow) The Seventeenth Congress of the Soviet Communist Party opened yesterday at the Kremlin. More than two thousand delegates attended, representing party departments across the federation. When Stalin entered the hall, he was greeted with enthusiastic applause that lasted for quite some time. All the delegates rose to pay their respects, shouting loudly in acclamation. Molotov delivered the opening address, and amidst enthusiastic cheers, the congress elected the presidium, which included Stalin, Molotov, Kaganovich, Voroshilov, Ordzhonikidze, Kalinin, Kirov, Kossior, Postyshev, and Lenin's widow. Subsequently, Stalin presented a report on behalf of the Central Executive Committee, which was again met with enthusiastic applause. The report lasted for five hours and was repeatedly interrupted by applause. At the conclusion of the report, there was a long period of applause, followed by the congress delegates singing the Internationale. (TASS dispatch of the 27th) (Moscow) Molotov, representing the Central Committee of the Communist Party of the Soviet Union, delivered the opening address at the congress, stating, "Since the last congress established the development of a force to thoroughly eliminate capitalist elements as the primary goal, a relatively short period has passed in an instant. During these years, the intense struggle of the working class against socialism has never ceased, and our socialist construction has achieved tremendous victories. Our party, under the banner of developing offensive forces, has united the working class and the peasant masses, leading them to thoroughly complete the aforementioned goals. Despite the croaking of our enemies predicting the inevitable failure of the Five-Year Plan, our party was able to complete it thoroughly within four years. All the great industries in our country today, along with their installed technology and the machines they can produce, will in the future be able to manufacture all products to meet the needs of various sectors of the national economy for technical equipment and to develop our national defense capabilities." The Second Five-Year Plan We have already launched the struggle to realize the Second Five-Year Plan. At this congress, regarding the Second Five-Year Plan, which is a five-year plan to build a socialist society without classes, we must make a final judgment. The convening of this congress coincides with the final victory of collective farming throughout the federation and the gradual elimination of rich peasant elements. Last year's unprecedented harvest is a testament to the great success of agriculture. An affluent and cultured life is already within reach, and tens of millions of collective farmers are beginning to realize this kind of life. We still have some problems to be solved. We still have backward economic sectors whose command of new technologies and industries is insufficient. However, it is evident that the Soviet state is always able to overcome all the difficulties it encounters and can continuously make rapid economic and cultural developments to bring greater prosperity to the working masses. The fundamental difference between the Soviet state, which is building socialism, and the bourgeoisie, which maintains the capitalist system, lies in this." Molotov on the Prosperity of the Soviet Economy Molotov contrasted the growing prosperity of the Soviet economy with the economic panic of capitalist countries, saying, "The facts of every day are sufficient to show the increasingly greater power of countless socialist forces in the Soviet Union. On the other hand, there is the world economic crisis and the increasingly surging revolutionary struggles of workers against capitalism and bourgeois dictatorship. These facts provide countless ironclad proofs of the impending collapse of the capitalist system of the bourgeoisie. The reason why the enthusiasm of socialist builders in our country is growing is also due to this. The working class and the masses of collective farmers express their special enthusiasm for the Seventeenth Congress of our party. All of this demonstrates the efforts and firm determination with which millions of workers and collective farmers are fighting for the complete victory of socialism in our country. The congress will mobilize the masses with new and higher standards, uniting them around the Bolshevik Party and around our victorious leader and organizer, Comrade Stalin." Molotov continued, "This congress will win enthusiastic responses in the hearts of millions of proletarians and oppressed peoples in countries outside the Soviet Union. We tell them that our struggle to win the victory of socialism is inextricably linked to the anti-capitalist revolution of workers around the world. Preparing for a Pressing Opportunity Molotov further stated, "In recent years, we have considered the necessity of an increasingly pressing war crisis in many situations. At present, especially regarding the situation in the Far East, we must strengthen our vigilance and preparation to safeguard the great victory of the October Revolution. While we resolutely pursue a policy of peace and promote peaceful cooperation with other countries, at the same time, we must pay special attention to strengthening the combat power of our glorious Red Army. The convening of this congress coincides with the tenth anniversary of the death of Lenin, the great leader and organizer of our party and the socialist revolution. Only by relying on the revitalization of Lenin's legacy and the implementation of Lenin's policies can our party achieve great victories. The greatest contribution to the implementation of Lenin's legacy in practice is our Central Committee, and Comrade Stalin, the faithful successor of Lenin's policies, is the leader of the Central Committee. Solving the problems of struggle and organization in socialist construction and strengthening the party's leadership in construction work are the most important issues of the congress," he said. If any omissions or concealments are found, the county magistrate shall be severely punished, and the district, township, and village chiefs who are jointly responsible shall also be dismissed and punished, in order to eliminate the evil thoroughly. The Current Situation of Anti-Japanese Resistance in Jilin's Jiandao (2) 80

Jilin Correspondence

In the previous correspondence, I briefly introduced the history of Jiandao, the establishment of the so-called anti-Japanese "People's Revolutionary Government," and the general anti-Japanese organizations in the area. Now, I will further describe the area of the organization and the situation of the Japanese and puppet troops as follows: The six locations of Wangyugou, Shirengou, Hualianli, Changrengou, Dongzigou within Yanji County of Jilin, and Sisuping within Wangqing County are all so-called People's Revolutionary Government areas. Although these locations are close to major cities, they are all mountainous areas that are not easy to attack, and because the locations are interconnected, if the Japanese and puppet troops attack one place, they can escape to another. The base is in Wangyugou, and the headquarters of the Eastern Manchurian Special Committee is located here. Last November, the Japanese army sent troops to attack. At that time, some areas were indeed completely swept away. However, in December, when the Japanese army retreated, they rose up again and continued to carry out their work in the area. When the Japanese army goes there, it must mobilize a large number of troops; otherwise, not only will military equipment be confiscated, but the soldiers will also not be able to return.

The Japanese and puppet troops have launched attacks many times, but they are not afraid of this, and they have made considerable preparations in advance, so the Japanese and puppet troops cannot easily succeed. In fact, the area only occupies a few dozen li near Juzi Street. However, within this area, people who oppose the government are not allowed to take a step without authorization. Strict guard networks are set up everywhere. Last August, a Japanese couple working along the South Manchuria Railway line mistakenly entered the area and were detained for more than a month before being released. After returning, they talked about the situation in the area, saying, "At first, we thought we would be killed, but after the party cadres found out that we were indeed lost people and not spies, they treated us very well. Finally, they escorted us to the border and solemnly said, 'This is our national border. We do not allow anyone to arbitrarily enter our territory, nor do we arbitrarily enter other people's territory. Please convey this message to others after you return.'"

Looking at the above, one can understand the seriousness of their defense of the area. On the border of the area, sentries are stationed day and night. If they see Japanese and puppet troops coming to attack, the first line of sentries will throw homemade explosive bombs to notify the sentries on the mountain. The message is passed from one to two, and from two to three, and then reported to the headquarters. In an instant, everyone escapes into the dense forest in the mountains. If the Japanese and puppet troops attack at night, they light a fire on the top of the mountain, and the signal is transmitted from this mountain to that mountain by means of beacon fire, notifying the headquarters, and they flee to the predetermined location together. Armed personnel resist the Japanese and puppet troops, trying to concentrate the Japanese and puppet troops in one place so that other personnel can take the opportunity to escape, while they retreat along a predetermined path, and fight as they retreat, eventually causing outsiders to retreat without understanding the path. Armed party members only take the guns of the fallen party members, and abandon their bodies, because they value weapons more than human corpses. When escaping, they all tightly bind their leggings, carry daily necessities, and food that can last for six or seven days, making a home wherever they go. When they see the Japanese army coming, they escape to another place. They are familiar with the mountain roads, as if they are walking in their own houses, and they will not get lost no matter how winding the path is. What is left in the villages are only the elderly, weak, women, and children. The Japanese Consulate General Police Yilangou Sub-station is stationed more than ten li outside Wangyugou, the central area of the government. From May to November last year, it fought with the nearby army as many as 87 times. The first line of sentries of the government is on the top of the mountain six li away from the Yilangou Japanese police station.

As for bullets and gunpowder, it is said that they are self-made. The manufacturer is a Korean old man in his sixties who used to be a technician in an arms manufacturing factory. His name is Guo Xiangxue. He privately manufactured ammunition in the deep mountains of Hamgyongnam-do in Korea and participated in the independence movement. After that, he took refuge in Liuhe County, Liaoning, and continued to manufacture gunpowder guns and bullets, and participated in various independence movements. Last August, he was summoned by the government and is now manufacturing bullets and explosives with two assistants in an underground room in Wangyugou for the government.

When the Japanese army attacked, they burned down houses and huts to cut off their return route. Wangyugou and other places were almost completely swept away, but they soon returned in formation and started working. They live a life of escaping in the deep mountains, sleeping in the grass in summer and digging holes to live together in winter, gathering five or six people in one hole, some of which even contain printing presses, so they do not forget their work even in a life of escape.

Although they try to preserve their strength, the population has inevitably decreased due to the repeated attacks and deaths by the Japanese and puppet troops. In order to expand their influence and work, they are trying their best to lure Korean farmers and railway workers to join the anti-Japanese work, and distribute land to them for cultivation, and when necessary, they also make them join in resisting foreign enemies or transporting items.

Recently, in order to further consolidate the foundation of the government area, they have changed from the previous direct action, and now carry out organization, propaganda, and riot work simultaneously. All people within the territory need to be monitored by armed party members, restricting their freedom and strictly preventing them from defecting to the Japanese and puppet troops. In order to prepare for the winter, party cadres strictly prohibit the export of autumn harvested grains outside the area. Anyone who violates this order is not only considered a counter-revolutionary, but is also punished on the spot.

Between February and November of last year, the Japanese and puppet authorities organized the "Jiandao Communist Bandit Surrender Review Committee." It is said that more than a thousand people went to surrender. These are mostly Korean farmers and natives who have lived in the deep mountains of Jiandao for a long time, who do not know who owns the land they live on, and do not know what the Soviet Union or Japan is. They only know how to cultivate when the sun rises and rest when the sun sets, and they cultivate all day long for warmth and a full stomach.

Recently, the Japanese and puppet authorities have been trying their best to attack, using both military force and political means. Therefore, the Jiandao Map Security Maintenance Association and the Manchukuo Concord Association Jiandao Local Affairs Bureau have been established. While coordinating with military police and other agencies, military force and politics are carried out simultaneously, so the fate of this organization cannot be predicted. (The End)

The West Route Army Will Complete Its Mission 81

Liu Jianxu Stationed in Lianhua to Vigorously Suppress the Xiao Bandits

Liu Yinggu Stationed in Wanzai to Supervise the Suppression of the Kong Bandits

Changsha Correspondence: After He Jian took office as the Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression Army of the Jiangxi-Guangdong-Fujian-Hunan-Hubei West Route, he commanded fourteen divisions and two independent brigades to suppress the Red bandits in the Jiangxi West, Jiangxi North, Hubei South, and Hunan East areas. For several months, the bandit areas have been shrinking day by day. The bandits in the Western Route only have two major groups: Xiao Ke and Kong Hechong, with a total of no more than 30,000 guns. They have been severely suppressed by the Western Route and have suffered heavy losses in dozens or hundreds of battles, large and small. Important bandit nests have also been captured by the National Army. Here is a detailed description of the recent situation of the Xiao and Kong bandits: The Situation of the Xiao Bandits

The Xiao bandits are the strongest in Jiangxi West, with about 20,000 guns and twice as many people. They have been entrenched in the Lianhua, Ninggang, and Yongxin areas for the longest time, and from time to time they invade the counties of Chaling, Youxian, and Liling in Hunan East, and Pingxiang in Jiangxi. The task of the Western Route Army to suppress bandits is to target the Xiao bandits as its biggest goal. After the establishment of the Western Route Army in June last year, He Jian sent Liu Jianxu, the commander of the 28th Army and the commander of the First Column of the Western Route Army, to lead the 15th Division of Wang Dongyuan, the 16th Division of Peng Weiren, and the 63rd Division of Chen Guangzhong to advance from Chaling to Lianhua, Ninggang, and Yongxin to suppress the bandits. In August, the Ninggang was recovered by Wang Dongyuan's division. In October, Lianhua was recovered by Chen Guangzhong's division. However, both Ninggang and Lianhua counties have been captured by bandits for six years and have been deeply infiltrated by bandits. Although the county towns have been recovered, the bandits still entrenched in the surrounding villages. After two or three months of suppression, the villages and towns were completely recovered until December. Liu Jianxu then moved from Chaling to Lianhua and continued to advance towards the Yongxin bandit nest. It has been found that Yongxin is the base of the Xiao bandits, with a large area and the danger of Qixi Ridge and Meihua Mountain. The Xiao bandits occupy it as a nest. Liu Jianxu used the method of advancing step by step with the three divisions to encircle Yongxin. Because the National Army was pressing closer and closer, Yongxin was afraid that it would be difficult to hold out for long, so it implemented a plan to abandon the old nest and develop a new Soviet area, moving its strength to attack Anfufu and leaving only the guard division, the Red Army School, and an independent regiment of about 2,000 to 3,000 people to defend Meihua Mountain. Peng Weiren's 16th Division launched an attack on January 11 this year, braving the snow. After fierce fighting until dawn on the 13th, Liu Jiren's brigade occupied the General Mountain, Wufu Temple, Meihua Mountain, and other important positions. The bandits retreated to Yongxin. Peng's division is now chasing to the outside of Yongquan City and encircling it, and it can be recovered soon. At the same time, the main force of the Xiao bandits surrounded Anfu on the 10th. Only one regiment of troops was stationed in the city, closing the city and defending it to wait for reinforcements. Liu Jianxu reported and ordered part of Peng's division and Wang Dongyuan's division to rush to aid. It is expected that they can arrive on the 23rd or 24th. Anfu has been besieged for half a month. After the reinforcements arrive, there will be a fierce battle in Anfu. According to the captured bandits, the Xiao bandits had three intentions for attacking Anfu: 1. They can cross east to join the pseudo-135th Army Group. 2. They can establish contact with the Kong bandits. 3. They can attack Ji'an and obtain a central location in the Gan River. However, judging from the situation, the old nest of the Xiao bandits, Yongxin, will inevitably be lost and can be captured sooner or later, and the new Soviet area of ​​Anfu County that they are trying to obtain is now being aided by reinforcements, and it will be difficult to obtain it. Even if it can be captured, Anfu is an area of ​​four battles and has no important risks to defend. There is also a highway to Ji'an that can be passed, and it is a place where the Northwest and West Route armies can attack from both sides, so it is difficult to occupy it for a long time. Therefore, the current situation of the Xiao bandits will inevitably lead to a wandering existence.

The Situation of the Kong Bandits 82

Kong Hechong only has more than 10,000 guns, and his strength is not as strong as that of the Xiao bandits. He has been disrupting the Pingjiang and Liuyang areas of Hunan East, the Xiushui, Wanzai, Tonggu, and Pingxiang areas of Jiangxi Northwest, and the Chongyang and Tongcheng areas of Hubei South for six or seven years. The intensity of the damage is the worst of all the bandits. After the establishment of the West Route Army, He Jian ordered Chen Jicheng, commander of the Third Column, to send troops to block the Chongtong area of ​​Hubei South, and Li Jue's 19th Route Army to be stationed in the Pingliu area of ​​Hunan East to block the bandits. He also sent the 18th Division of Zhu Yaohua, the 50th Division of Yue Sen, and the 62nd Division of Tao Guang, which belong to the Second Column, to take charge of suppressing the bandits. After half a year of suppression, they successively recovered the county towns of Xiushui, Tonggu, and Wanzai and gradually searched into the bandit area. The Kong bandits originally relied on the danger of two bandit nests, one is Gao Cun and the other is Xiao Yuan, both of which are under the jurisdiction of Wanzai County. The mountains are steep and not easy to enter. The Western Route Army spent a lot of effort and finally recovered Gao Cun by Tao Guangren's brigade last month. At present, the Kong bandits have fled into the Xiao Yuan bandit nest, relying on the danger and stubbornly resisting. The bandit area has been shrinking day by day. He Jian has sent Liu Yinggu, commander of the Second Column, to be stationed in Wanzai from Pingxiang a few days ago to supervise the advance of his troops towards the Xiao Yuan bandit nest, and ordered him to destroy the bandits in the shortest possible time.

Judging from the above situation, the bandit suppression situation of the West Route Army is gradually improving. He Jian reported in the memorial week that as long as the bandits in the North Route do not flee west, the mission of the West Route Army (that is, suppressing the Xiao and Kong bandits) can be completed in at most four months. However, the banditry in various places is too deep, and there is nothing left. The pacification and rehabilitation will still take a lot of effort. (January 24)

Major Theft at the Shan Zhai Library 83

Seventy-One Stolen Antiquities

The Case Solved, Returning Everything Intact

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong Provincial Library holds an extremely rich collection of ancient artifacts, bronze inscriptions, calligraphy, and paintings, which aroused the covetousness of bandits. On the twenty-first of this month, a shocking major theft occurred. The bandits entered by scaling the wall from the north along the telegraph poles and stole a total of seventy-one items from the ancient art exhibition room, including Song, Ming, and Qing dynasty porcelain, Han dynasty jade and bronze ware, and ancient book boxes. The library director, Wang Xiantang, recognizing the seriousness of the matter, reported it to the Department of Education and the Public Security Bureau and notified all parties to maintain strict secrecy in order to apprehend the bandits and recover the stolen items. In the days that followed, the Public Security Bureau dispatched detectives in disguise to investigate. On the evening of the twenty-fourth, the thief, Si Zhengming, returned to the reed ponds on the shore of Daming Lake in front of the library to retrieve five more porcelain plates and other items that he had hidden, but he was spotted and arrested by Zhao Shiqi, a patrol officer from the Second Police Station of the Third Branch of the city's Public Security Bureau. Today (the 25th), his home was searched, and his wife, Si Zhao, was arrested. Under strict interrogation, they confessed that the stolen artifacts were hidden in the tile ridges on the roof. The detective team recovered them, fortunately, all intact and without any losses. They have been reclaimed by the library. The Public Security Bureau believes that a theft of this magnitude could not have been carried out by one or two people alone, and investigations and interrogations are still ongoing. The details of the theft and its resolution are quite convoluted. The details of what happened are recorded below:

Discovery of the Theft: The theft of ancient artifacts from the Shandong Provincial Library occurred on the night of the twenty-first. That day was a Sunday, and the library was closed on Mondays, as usual. Most of the library staff went home in the evening or went out to play. Even those who returned to the library slept soundly. The thieves took advantage of this opportunity to carry out their scheme, scaling the wall and entering the premises at night, stealing as many as seventy-one ancient artifacts from the ancient art exhibition room. On Monday (the 22nd) morning, the library director, Wang Xiantang, got up early to inspect the premises and was surprised to see the door of the art exhibition room in the back courtyard wide open. Upon entering to investigate, he found the door damaged, the lock broken, and half of the ancient treasures missing. He knew it had been robbed. He inspected the courtyard and found a ladder leaning against the wall near the rockery in the northeast corner of the front courtyard, tied to a tree with a rope. On the ground, there was a Han dynasty ding (cauldron) containing several other small artifacts. This was evidently the thieves' entry and exit point. The Han ding was something they had been unable to carry away, and the ladder was the one used by the library to clean chimneys, which the thieves had moved after entering the premises.

Seventy-One Items: A detailed examination revealed that a total of seventy-one items were missing: (1) Porcelain: One sky-blue bottle (Qianlong), one belt-pierced bottle (Qianlong), one Longquan plate (Ming), one wucai (five-color) plate (Wanli), three celadon flower plates (Chenghua), two blue-and-white large fruit plates (Yongzheng), one Song white porcelain incense burner, one Song dragon incense burner, one qinghua (blue-and-white) pouring vessel (Xuande), one "dragon ball watching the sea" zun (Yongzheng), one Qianlong Jian ware wine ewer, one qingbai (bluish-white) plum blossom vase (Yongzheng), one wucai moon flask, one small Song zhi bottle with copper rim, three Ge ware plum blossom vases, eight large Jiajing yellow-glazed plates, one Ming Longquan plate, one Qianlong sky-blue plate, two large Chenghua painted flower bowls, one large Jiajing blue-and-white flower bowl, one Yongzheng wucai bowl, six red dragon sea bowls, two Qianlong rouge-red bowls, one Ming Longquan large fruit plate, one Tang porcelain jar; (2) Jade ware: one Han openwork jade cup, one Han jade bottle, one Han jade elephant-ear zun, one square zun, one flat flower vase, one jadeite garment pin, one Han jade chime, one Song jade chime; (3) Bronze ware: one Han hu (wine vessel) with yi (arrowhead) spout, one Zhou ding, one washing basin, four bronze mirrors, one Han yi (ewer), one Han dou (stemmed dish), one Han stele jade; (4) Books: two scrolls of Tang dynasty sutras, one volume of "Imperial Favorite: The Secret Method of Subduing Evil and Promoting Loyalty and Filial Piety," one volume of "Collected Works of Mr. Li of Wufeng," one volume of "Old Clouds Gathered at Gao Nanbu," one volume of "Pointing to the Moon with the South China Classic," one volume of "Seventeen Ancient Rhyme Manuals from the Yanshoujing Studio," one volume of "Han Shu Geography Index," and one volume of "Enping Travelogue." All seventy-one items are extremely precious and of immense value.

Detectives Sent Out: After discovering the theft, the library immediately reported the details of the robbery and the list of stolen artifacts to the Second Police Station of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau and requested the arrest of the perpetrators and the recovery of the stolen goods. It also reported the matter to the Department of Education. Before long, the Director of the Department of Education, He Siyuan, and the Director of the Public Security Bureau, Kai Ru, recognizing the gravity of the situation, arrived at the library one after another to inspect the scene. It was agreed that strict secrecy should be maintained in order to facilitate the investigation. Detectives were immediately dispatched to investigate the crime in disguise. The captain of the Special Detective Team, Liu Yaoting, also sent plainclothes officers to assist in the effort. However, the incident was strange, and there were initially no clues to be found. Therefore, plainclothes officers were deployed everywhere, both inside and outside Daming Lake near the library, as well as at the fire station and other places, to conduct thorough investigations. After two days, there were still no results.

The Thief Arrested: Yesterday (the 24th) at around 6 p.m., Zhao Shiqi, a patrol officer from the Second Police Station of the Third Branch of the city, disguised as a public official, was patrolling the mooring area on the small north-south road in Daming Lake, inside Huachiao. The dusk was deepening, and the cold wind chilled to the bone. There were no tourists to be seen. The patrol officer was lost in thought, still unable to find a clue, when he suddenly saw a middle-aged man walking along the lake embankment leading to the Lixia Pavilion, coming from north to south. He was carrying a quilt cover and a hook that looked like a hand tool, and his behavior was quite suspicious. The patrol officer took notice of him. When the man walked out of the gate leading into the lake, the patrol officer followed him. When he reached the western end of the Quehua Bridge, he hurriedly got into a rickshaw without bargaining and wanted to head west. The patrol officer immediately caught up and asked what was in the quilt cover. The man replied that it contained a few old books. When asked what else was inside, he appeared alarmed and stammered that there were also a few pieces of porcelain. The patrol officer became even more suspicious. At that moment, a guard from the Twenty-Seventh Watch Post of the Second Police Station of the Third Branch ordered an inspection. The man knew that he had been exposed, so he abandoned the quilt cover and fled in the direction from which he had come. The patrol officer joined the guard in a chase, pursuing him west along the newly constructed lakefront to the north of the library gate, where he was finally apprehended. The suspect resisted arrest with all his might, and the two sides fought hand-to-hand. However, he was outnumbered and eventually subdued. They returned to the Quehua Bridge and recovered the quilt cover he had abandoned, which contained five ancient plates that had been stolen from the library. They were immediately taken together to the Third Branch of the city's Public Security Bureau on Xiyan Gong Street, west of the Provincial Party Headquarters. Patrol Officer Zhao interrogated him first. He identified himself as Si Zhengming, 34 years old, from Pingyin County, Shandong Province, residing at No. 41 Houjie Street, Tongyuan Bureau. He had formerly been a member of the Communist Party and had served as an employee in the Communist Eradication Team after surrendering himself to the Provincial Party Headquarters. He had since been dismissed. He claimed that the five porcelain plates were what he had stolen and hidden in the lake, and he had only come to retrieve them tonight. He denied stealing anything else or having any accomplices.

Confessing the Truth: After the Third Branch solved the case, they detained the suspect at the bureau because it was already late. This morning (the 25th), they transferred him to the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, where he was interrogated once by the Judicial Section. The suspect's confession remained the same as the one he gave at the bureau. The General Bureau then ordered Tian Sirong, the director of the Third Branch, to bring officers, along with Deputy Team Leader Feng of the Special Affairs Team, to the suspect's home at No. 41 Houjie Street, Tongyuan Bureau, to conduct a search. Si Zhengming's wife, Si Zhao, strongly denied any knowledge of the stolen antiques. Deputy Team Leader Feng and others conducted a thorough search of the house but found nothing. Then, they saw Si Zhao hurriedly tearing a piece of paper into small pieces and stuffing them into her mouth. Feng and others immediately suspected something was amiss and demanded to know what she had swallowed. Si Zhao claimed it was a prescription. Seeing her evasive language, Feng and others seized the torn pieces of paper and pieced them together. It turned out to be a list of antiques she had made herself, with serial numbers. There was no doubt that all the other antiques had been stolen by them. However, after searching for a long time, they still found nothing. They took Si Zhao to the bureau for strict interrogation. Deputy Team Leader Feng then coaxed her, pretending to reassure her that she would be innocent if she told the truth, otherwise, her life would be in danger. Si Zhao believed him and confessed that all the stolen antiques were hidden in her home. She was willing to lead them home to unearth the loot. Deputy Team Leader Feng, Tian Sirong, Director of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau, and others accompanied Si Zhao to Si Zhengming's home to recover the stolen goods at 3 p.m.

Full Recovery of Stolen Goods: Deputy Team Leader Feng and his party arrived at Si Zhengming's home a second time, relying entirely on Si Zhao to direct their actions. In the west end of the north room, there was a women's toilet with a door next to it. A window was opened above the door. Deputy Team Leader Feng and others had found this suspicious during their initial inspection, but after searching, they found nothing. Now, Si Zhao led them to this location and told them that all the stolen antiques were hidden in the tiles on the roof outside the window. Deputy Team Leader Feng and others still could not find a way in. Under Si Zhao's guidance, they removed the tiles connecting to the neighbor's roof ridges. Suddenly, the entire batch of antiques appeared before them. Each item was wrapped in coarse paper. After counting and verifying, nothing was missing. Without someone to guide them, it would have been difficult to find this place. The precise arrangement was evident. The stolen goods were recovered. Deputy Team Leader Feng and others immediately carried them back to the General Bureau to report. They recounted them, and nothing was missing. Then, Director Wang Xiantang sent someone from the library to the bureau to check the items against the list and transport them back to the library. It was already 6 p.m.

Details of the Theft: The Public Security Bureau, with the evidence in hand and the case largely clarified, had Si Zhengming brought forward by the Judicial Section for strict interrogation. With the facts before him, Si Zhengming had no room for denial and confessed the entire course of his theft. He said that around 1 a.m. on the twenty-second, he climbed over the wall from the north side of the library gate along the telegraph poles. Inside the wall, there was a rockery made of flowers and stones, which was very close to the top of the wall. He climbed down from the rockery. Because the place was very close to the staff room, there was still light in the room, and he could hear the sound of someone taking medicine, so he did not dare to act at the time. He squatted in a secluded place to wait. It wasn't until 4 a.m. that he sneaked to the art exhibition room. The room had two doors, both of which were locked. He used the pliers he brought with him to break the locks, then entered the room, which was where the antiques were displayed. The antiques were displayed on shelves inside, and the shelves were also locked. He broke those locks as well, selected the valuable items, and wrapped them in coarse paper one by one. After packing them into one quilt cover and two willow baskets, he transported them to the wall where he had originally entered. He found a wooden ladder to help deliver the stolen items one by one over the wall with a rope. By this time, it was already after 6 a.m. Residents in the back street were already getting up early to work. Fearing that they would notice, he did not have time to transport one ding (cauldron) and left it inside the wall. The remaining items that had already been transported out were loaded onto a small boat and transported along the lake to the back of the Li Gong Temple, where they were then loaded onto a cart and transported home. However, five large plates were too heavy to transport at the time, so they were wrapped in a bundle and sunk in the lake. He only went to retrieve them last night (the 25th), and he was exposed because of these five plates, he said. (Twenty-fifth day)

Maritime Transportation Between Guangdong and Fujian Resumes 84

Situation in Fujian After the 19th Route Army Initially Withdraws

Shantou Correspondence: When the central government used force against Fujian, the Shantou Customs, under the order of the Inspector General of Customs, temporarily detained electric-powered and sailing ships traveling to and from Fujian, implementing a maritime blockade policy against the Fujian side. For a time, freight transport was suspended, and transportation between Fujian and Guangdong relied entirely on land routes. One route went from Shantou to Chenghai Zhanglin, then turned to Huanggang and entered Zhao'an. The other route went from Dabu to Yongding. In terms of distance, Shantou to Zhao'an could be reached in six hours, but in Huanggang, one had to travel eighteen li on an unfinished highway, and then reach Fenshui Pass to take a car to Zhao'an City. If one was familiar with the route and the language, this route could be a shortcut to Fujian. However, the road from Zhao'an to Yunxiao had to pass through Erdu. This highway had its bridges demolished when Zhang Zhen withdrew his troops the year before, and there were no cars running to this day. Moreover, there were many bandits along the way. If one could reach Yunxiao, there would be cars going directly to Zhangzhou, which would take about two hours. The 19th Route Army did not station troops in Yunxiao, Pinghe, or Zhao'an. The public order in these areas was poor. In the past, passengers and goods traveling to and from the area had to be escorted by the local militia and reserve forces. Now, it is regarded as a dangerous route.

After the 19th Route Army retreated to southern Fujian, their troops were distributed in the area from Qingyang below Jinjiang South Gate to Anhai Shitou, with about one regiment stationed there. One regiment was also stationed in Shishi Weitou, Tong'an, and Jimei. One regiment was stationed along the Zhangsong line of Shimei Haicang Songyu. One regiment was stationed along the Zhangfu line of Haicheng Shima Fugong. The main force was stationed near Quanzhou and Zhangzhou. The 19th Route Army had strict security measures along the Songzhang and Songzhangfu lines, with fortifications built at strategic locations. Li Jishen and Chen Mingshu were also in Zhangzhou, Jiang Guangnai was in Tong'an, and Cai Tingkai was in Quanzhou. Jiang, Cai, and Chen were prepared to each take charge of one of three fronts of combat. On the central government side, Zhang Zhi led the central army to attack Putian and Xianyou, Zhao Qintao attacked Datian and Dehua, and Jiang Dingwen transported troops by sea to Xiamen to take charge of attacking Zhangzhou. How the battles on these three fronts are unfolding, we have not yet received details here. Maritime transportation has resumed in recent days. The Haiyang, Haining, Haicheng, and Haishun ships, which passed through Fuzhou and Xiamen to Shantou and Hong Kong, sailed on the fifteenth, seventeenth, nineteenth, and twenty-first, respectively. These four ships were filled with people from military and political circles. The first- and second-class cabins were completely full. There were also more than a thousand passengers on the large ships. All the passengers returning to Shantou by ship changed to boats and cars to enter the inland areas of Chao'an or Jieyang immediately after disembarking. They did not stop in Shantou for trade, as if it had been arranged in advance. When asked about the recent situation in Fujian, everyone was tight-lipped. It was said that when they passed through Xiamen on the twentieth, the Xiamen authorities did not allow passengers to disembark. Those who transferred to Gulangyu to inquire about the news learned that Fugong and Songyu had been occupied by the central army. The Wanxiang and Tunan and other China Merchants Steam Navigation Company ships carrying troops had already unloaded military supplies. Two central naval vessels were protecting the ships. (Twenty-first)

Red Pill Manufacturing Den Discovered Outside Suzhou's Changmen Gate 85

At No. 41 Xiaozhu Lane outside Changmen Gate, someone was secretly setting up a red pill manufacturing den. After someone informed the Public Security Bureau's Third Branch, yesterday (the 27th) at 10 a.m., the bureau dispatched patrol officers and several policemen to conduct a search. After six hours of secret investigation, they finally found a red pill manufacturing machine, ten bags of red pills, several bags of raw materials such as sugar powder, ten liang of opium, dozens of liang of ingredients, and several bundles of Shuangshi (Double Lion) brand and Shiqiu (Lion Ball) brand red pill wrapping paper in the back garden. Several dozen wholesale ledgers and several invoice stamps were also found. The red pill manufacturing worker, Li Huanyun, and an employee were taken to the bureau together. According to Li's confession, the boss who manufactured the red pills had already fled. The manufactured red pills were sold to this city and various villages, as well as to neighboring Wuxi County and other places, which also came to buy wholesale, and so on.

Thugs Break into Home in Wuxi, Chopping and Killing Elderly Woman 86

Chen Tingkun, 55, the owner of Chen Tingji Woodworks in Li Lane outside Ximen Gate, had a wife named Huang, 57, and had one son and three daughters. The son, named Peikun, was already married. The eldest daughter, Cuixia, 22, was married to the Hu family in Yanqiao. The second daughter, Cuiyun, 18, was betrothed to the Jiang family but had not yet moved in. The youngest daughter, Amo, 13, was studying at school. However, Cuiyun was romantic and good at socializing. On the night before (the 26th) at about 9 p.m., Chen Huang, along with her youngest daughter, Amo, and her nephew, Huang Yunlun (8 years old), were sleeping in the front room. At about 11 p.m., a thug suddenly entered from the window, wielding an axe and aiming it at Chen Huang's head, chopping down three times with full force. Blood splattered everywhere, and brain matter burst out. After Chen Huang felt the pain, her legs thrashed wildly. Amo, shocked, looked up and saw her mother on her last breaths. She shouted loudly for help. By this time, the thug had already fled. The family members, hearing the sound, woke up in shock. They immediately carried the injured woman to Tongren Hospital for treatment. However, because her skull had been shattered and she had lost too much blood, it was too late to save her, and she died immediately. The next day, Fan Xin, the director of the Fourth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, personally went to investigate and recovered an axe left behind by the killer. He took the two daughters, Cuiyun and Amo, to the bureau for questioning. At the same time, Chen Zizhao, the chief of Nian Er Tu, reported to the County Court, requesting an autopsy as proof for handling the case.

Sudden Conflict Arises Among Police and Local Militia 87

Police officer Shi Xiaoming (from Guangxi) of the Third Station of the Public Security Bureau's Third Branch, while on duty at the Jingqiao checkpoint in his jurisdiction on the evening before (the 26th) at about 8 p.m., encountered a patrol from the Fifth Squad of the local militia passing by. The police officer was slightly slow in saluting, and the militia suspected that he was intentionally showing disrespect, so they questioned him. A conflict arose between them, and the militia injured the police officer. Officer Shi, feeling insulted, immediately ran back to the bureau and reported the situation to Branch Director Mao. At the same time, all the police officers in the bureau, upon hearing the news, were indignant and unanimously left their posts. Subsequently, Patrol Leaders Long Baoda and Xu Zhian led several police officers to the headquarters of the Fifth Squad of the militia to invite Squad Leader Guo to the bureau for talks. Unexpectedly, the militia misunderstood, suspecting that the police officers had come to retaliate, so the order was disrupted for a time. During the turmoil, the equipment in the squad headquarters was slightly damaged. Later, Xu Yi, the winter defense director of the county government, as well as Li Wengong, the director of the Public Security Bureau, and Inspector General Wei Yu mediated. However, the two sides reported their respective grievances, making it difficult to resolve the situation. It was subsequently decided to report the situation to the county government for the county magistrate to provide instructions before determining a resolution. The police officers of the Third Branch have already returned to their posts as a whole and are awaiting orders from their superiors.

Fire in City and Countryside Claims Lives 88

Jin, the wife of Ren Dabao, a villager in Chen Douban Lane, Liu Tan Bridge South (Tianxia Market) in the Sixth District of the county, returned from chanting Buddhist scriptures at the Dongping Wang Temple nearby on the previous evening and went to bed. Unexpectedly, she accidentally knocked over the foot warmer, causing it to burn the bedding. Jin was unable to escape and was buried in the fire. It took about half an hour to extinguish the fire, but five houses had already been completely destroyed. Also, at Wufeng Candle Shop in Bu Lane outside the North Gate, a fire suddenly broke out at 3 a.m. yesterday (the 27th). The entire shop, with its two bays and three buildings, was completely destroyed, with losses estimated at more than 1,000 yuan.

Kunshan Detective Team Arrests Qidong Bandits 89

In mid-September of last year, the Dacheng Flower Shop in Nanyang Village, Qidong County, was robbed by bandits of 6,000 yuan in banknotes and silver dollars, and an old clerk was shot and killed. Wang Yunshan, the captain of the county's detective team, arrested Wu Changqing, one of the bandits in this case, in Shanghai and confiscated 100 yuan in banknotes. He was immediately brought back for questioning. According to his confession, the crime was committed together with Shi Zhaolin, Zhou Xiaodi, and others who were still at large. Yesterday, Captain Wang arrested Shi Cai'gen, the younger brother of Shi Zhaolin, in Shanghai. He immediately submitted him to the county government, awaiting the county's dispatch of police to escort him back for investigation.

Patrol Officer Accepts Bribe, Releases Large Shipment of Red Pills 90

Yan Chuntang, a drug dealer, obtained more than 1,200 jin of Jinji (Golden Rooster) brand red pills in Shanghai the day before and shipped them to Wuxi for sale by boat. When passing through the Datong Bridge in Pengjian Town in this county, Jiang Zhen, a patrol officer from the local Public Security Sub-Station, learned of this and immediately sent police to detain the boat. Later, Yan paid a bribe of 1,300 yuan to redeem the boat and the red pills, which continued on to Wuxi for sale. This matter was discovered by Hua Shijun, the director of the County Public Security Bureau, who was greatly angered and sent Wen Zongxin, the director of the relevant sub-bureau, to conduct a secret investigation yesterday morning.

Zhenjiang Rickshaw Pullers Launch General Strike 91

The rickshaw pullers in Zhenjiang, due to demands for rent reductions and requests to eliminate the joint operation of buses, started a work slowdown. Yesterday, it suddenly affected everyone, and the situation became serious. Because they could not eat on days they did not pull, they all hoped that the authorities would quickly respond to their demands. Unexpectedly, the authorities ignored them. Therefore, the rickshaw pullers' families went out to prevent the joint operation buses of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway and the Zhenjiang-Yangzhou Company from passing through. Xiang Zhizhuang, the director of the Security Office, in an attempt to quickly resolve the situation, summoned rickshaw puller representatives Fang Yuanhong and others for talks, promising to respond the same day. Lu Xiaobo, chairman of the Standing Committee of the Chamber of Commerce, also convened all the rickshaw shop owners at the Chamber of Commerce yesterday to discuss the issue of rent reduction. More than ten people, including Cao Liqing and Yang Dianba, attended. After talking for over an hour, no satisfactory solution was reached. Because of cost considerations, the rickshaw shop owners insisted that they could not reduce the rent. The rickshaw pullers had no choice but to gather again at the station, forcibly preventing the joint operation buses from passing through. The military police tried their best to persuade them, and no incident occurred. However, the Chamber of Commerce, fearing that the situation would escalate, has sent a letter to Zeng Zhihong, the stationmaster of Zhenjiang Station, to forward it to the Railway Bureau, requesting that the joint operation be postponed to avoid affecting the livelihoods of the rickshaw pullers during this cold winter. We do not know how the Railway Bureau will handle it. In recent days, no rickshaws have been seen on the streets, causing great inconvenience for passengers getting on and off at the station and the wharves along the river. Pedestrians are lamenting that they cannot travel.

Changzhou County Chamber of Commerce Representative Assembly 92

The Wuyi County Chamber of Commerce convened a representative assembly on the twenty-sixth. More than 120 representatives of the members, including Xu Juxi, attended. Huang Gongwang, an instructor from the county party headquarters, and Zhang Bing, a supervisor from the county government, were present. After Chairman Xu Juxi gave a report, half of the original fifteen executive committee members were removed. In addition to the revocation of qualification of executive committee member Shen Yuanduo, six people, including Xu Fukang, Li Furen, Cha Bangyan, Gao Zhen, Liu Guojun, and Liu Yaoxing, were removed. Three of the seven supervisory committee members had either died or had their qualifications revoked, which was exactly half, so no further drawing was needed. Then, the proposals were discussed. Representatives from the party and government agencies gave speeches, and Xu Juxi gave a response. The meeting adjourned. The supplementary election of officials will be held on the twenty-eighth.

Wufeng Candle Shop in Bu Lane outside the North Gate, a fire suddenly broke out at 3 a.m. yesterday (the 27th). The entire shop, with its two bays and three buildings, was completely destroyed, with losses estimated at more than 1,000 yuan.

The Municipal Party Headquarters Holds an Assembly of All Sectors.

The National Society Reports: Today is the Anniversary of the Tragic Anti-Japanese Resistance of the National Revolutionary Army in Songhu Two Years Ago. The Municipal Party Headquarters Has Issued a Notice Convening Representatives from All Sectors of the City to Hold the "Shanghai All-Sectors Assembly Commemorating the Second Anniversary of the Songhu National Revolutionary Army's Anti-Japanese Resistance on January 28th" at the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Group at 9:00 AM Today. It is Also Scheduled That, Starting at 11:00 AM Today, All Citizens Will Observe Three Minutes of Silence to Express Deep Mourning for the Anti-Japanese Martyrs and Compatriots Who Perished. Due to Concerns That Reactionary Elements Might Take the Opportunity to Cause Trouble, the Police Authorities of Various Sectors in the Chinese Concessions of This City Have Implemented Strict Security Measures. The Seventh District Party Headquarters Convened Representatives from All Sectors to Commemorate and Offer Public Sacrifices in the Jiangwan Area Due to Its Distance from the City. The Situation is Recorded Below:

Arrangement of the Venue:

The Venue is Located at the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Group (Contrary to What Was Reported in Yesterday's Newspaper About the Municipal Chamber of Commerce). A White Cloth Banner Hangs in Front of the Door, Reading "Shanghai All-Sectors Assembly Commemorating the Second Anniversary of the Songhu National Revolutionary Army's Anti-Japanese Resistance on January 28th." In the Center of the Auditorium, the Party and National Flags and the Portrait of the Premier are Hung. Order Slogans are Pasted on Both Sides, and Slogans Cover the Four Walls. The Arrangement is Very Solemn.

Assembly Staff:

The Assembly is Convened by a Notice from the Municipal Party Headquarters. The Presidium is Scheduled to Consist of Xing Wan of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Wu Tiecheng of the Municipal Government, Yang Hu of the Municipal Security Department, Wang Xiaolai of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Zhu Xuefan of the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, Yu Zhenhui of the Municipal Farmers' Association, and Xue Guangqian of the University Students' Federation, Among Seven Others. The Master of Ceremonies is Zhang Hanyun. The Recorders are Tong Muge and Du Mengsen. The Hosts are Huang Xianggu, Huang E, Li Erbai, Zhu Xiaochun, Fan Mingyao, and Lai Zhiwen. The Order Keepers are Lin Kecong, Cao Runshen, Wang Guoping, and Bao Huizhong. The Public Security Bureau Military Band Will Attend to Play Music, and the Security Team and Police Will Maintain Order at the Venue.
