Notice: This Association is Scheduled to Convene Representatives from All Sectors of This City at the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Group at 9:00 AM on January 28th to Hold the Second Anniversary Commemorative Assembly for the Songhu National Revolutionary Army's Anti-Japanese Resistance. This Notice is Specifically Issued in the Hope That All Agencies, Organizations, Schools, and Party Headquarters at All Levels in This City Will Send Four Representatives with Letters to Attend. This is of Utmost Importance and is Hereby Notified.

Letter to the People:

The Municipal Party Headquarters' Letter to the People Commemorating the Second Anniversary of the "January 28th" Songhu Anti-Japanese Resistance (Excerpt Above): Today, Two Years Ago, Is the Anniversary of the Japanese Imperialists' Massacre of the Shanghai People with Airplanes and Cannons. It is Also the Most Painful Anniversary for Our Entire Republic of China After "September 18th," Suffering from the Invasion and Oppression of Japanese Warlords. More Than Two Years Have Passed Since the Incident. The Ashes of the Songhu Disaster Remain as Before, and This Great National Shame and Deep Hatred Has Not Only Not Been Erased, but Has Become Increasingly Serious. How Heartbreaking This Is. What Makes Us Especially Sad Today Is That the 19th Route Army, Which Once Boasted of "Guns Pointing Outward and Never Inward" and Contributed to the War, Now Does Not Cherish Itself and Colludes with Japan in Fujian to Suppress Communists, Committing Acts of Destroying the Party and Betraying the Country. The Former Pain Lies in Foreign Aggression, and the Latter Pain Lies in Internal Trouble. Foreign Aggression Without Internal Trouble Can Sometimes Be Erased, but the Occurrence of Internal Trouble Directly Exacerbates Foreign Aggression. Therefore, If We Do Not Want to Save the Country, Then So Be It. If We Want to Save This Perilous Country, We Must First Address What Is Urgent and Then Whip What Is Not Urgent. In Other Words, We Must First Pacify the Interior and Then Repel Foreign Aggressors (Middle Excerpt). In the Past, the 19th Route Army Only Took the Opportunity to Steal the Name of Patriotism as a Cover for Deceiving the People. As of Today, When the Fujian Incident Occurred, Its True Colors Were Finally Exposed. Therefore, All Truly Patriotic Soldiers Must Always Be Under the Central Government's Control to Maintain the Party and the Country in Order to Survive and Obtain National Protection. Otherwise, Seeking Temporary False Fame and Trying to Achieve One's Ambitions Will Ultimately Fail. This Is Why the 19th Route Army, Which Incited Chaos in Fujian Today, Collapsed in an Instant. Furthermore, In the Battle of Songhu, Our Army's Combat Power Was Not Up to Par. However, the Enemy Ultimately Used Airplanes to Bombard Us, Causing Us to Be Unable to Withstand It and Retreat. We Deeply Learned from the Lessons of the Past. Therefore, During the First Anniversary Commemoration Last Year, We Held National Air Defense Propaganda. Over the Past Year, It Has Been Very Effective. Now, the Lost Territory in the Northeast Has Not Been Recovered, and the International Situation is Becoming Increasingly Urgent. The Difficulties of Tomorrow Are Just Beginning. Therefore, When We Commemorate "January 28th," We Should Continue to Expand the Work of Air Defense and Strengthen the Air Force's Strength in Time to Prepare for Self-Defense, Which Is to Unite to Erase the National Shame in the Future (Bottom Excerpt).

A Glimpse of Slogans:

(1) January 28th is a Day for the Brutal Sun to Invade Songhu and the Chinese People to Resist. (2) January 28th is a Day to Demonstrate the Spirit of the Chinese Nation. (3) Promote the Spirit of the Songhu National Revolutionary Army's Rising Up to Resist the Enemy on January 28th. (4) Compatriots Across the Country Unite to Expand the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Movement. (5) Compatriots Across the Country Unite to Realize Air Defense. (6) Vow to Implement Economic Severance, Boycott Enemy Goods, and Promote National Products. (7) Down with Japanese Imperialism. (8) Erase the Humiliation of January 28th. (9) Recover the Lost Territory in the Northeast. (10) Long Live the Republic of China.

Citywide Alert:

In Order to Prevent Reactionary Elements from Causing Trouble, the Municipal Party Headquarters Specially Sent a Letter to the Garrison Headquarters and the Municipal Public Security Bureau to Announce Martial Law. It Was Reported That the Garrison Department, the Municipal Security Department, and the Municipal Public Security Bureau Had Ordered Their Subordinates Several Days Ago to Dispatch Soldiers and Police to Guard Posts and Increase Patrols. They Also Sent Detectives, Inspectors, and Male and Female Inspectors to Important Locations to Implement Security and Inspect Pedestrians. The Vicinity of Various Agencies Was Under Especially Strict Security. The Police Departments of the Two Concessions Also Added Detectives to the Vicinity of Various Agencies, Factories, and the Border Between the Chinese and Foreign Concessions to Prevent Trouble from Spreading.

Public Sacrifice in Jiangwan:

The Jiangwan Seventh District Party Headquarters of This City, Due to Being Far From Shanghai, Specially Presented to the Municipal Party Headquarters to Convene Representatives From All Sectors in Jiangwan, Yinxiang, Yinhang, and Other Places at 9:00 AM Today in the Department's Auditorium to Hold a Commemorative Assembly. After the Meeting, All Representatives Will Go to the "January 28th" Martyrs' Cemetery in Changgou Bay, Jiangwan Garden Road, to Offer Public Sacrifices to Show Commemoration.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Issues a Commemorative Declaration. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Issued a Commemorative Declaration for January 28th:

As the Saying Goes, "One Suffers Once, One Learns a Lesson." This, Although a Vulgar Saying From the Lower Class, Actually Contains the Ultimate Truth of Protecting the Country and the Home. The Songhu Blood Battle Left Scars That Are Still Fresh. Every Compatriot With a Little Blood and Knowledge Should Regard This Painful and Tragic Piece of History as a Deeply Engraved Lesson. This Certainly Does Not Require Our Redundancy. However, Merely Not Forgetting the National Crisis and Encouraging Oneself and Others Has Limited Effect. One Must Be Determined to Immerse Oneself in Hard Work to Have a Day to Escape the Sea of ​​Suffering and Reach the Other Shore. This Association Now Has a Word to Offer to Compatriots in Shanghai. If Someone Asks How to Compensate for the Loss of 140,000 Citizens of Shanghai in the Songhu Battle, Everyone Will Hesitate and Be Unable to Answer. However, This Association Believes That the Way to Compensate Lies in the Citizens Themselves. If Everyone is Determined to Swear That From Now On, They Will Not Use Anything Other Than National Products for Food, Clothing, and All Consumption, Then With Shanghai's Large Population and High Standard of Living, They Can Reduce the Annual Loss of 100 Million, and the Entire Loss of the Songhu Battle Can Be Compensated for in the Next Fourteen Years. This is the Most Practical Method of Subduing Others Without Fighting and Seeking Solutions Within Oneself. It Is Also the Saying "One Suffers Once, One Learns a Lesson." Otherwise, If a Son of a Wealthy Family Conspires to Seize His Inheritance With His Neighbor, and the Unfilial Son Still Privately Conspires With Money, He Will End Up With Nothing to Stand On. Now is the Critical Moment of Success or Failure. Compatriots Can Choose for Themselves.

The National Product Factory Jointly Issues a Letter to Compatriots:

The National News Agency Reports: The Chinese National Product Manufacturers Association Today Issued a January 28th Letter to All Sisters: "Sisters, You Can't All Be Unpatriotic People, Can You? You Can't All Be People Without Blood, Can You? We Often Have an Ideal That Comforts Ourselves, 'Chinese People Are Patriotic, How Can They Not Be United? Perhaps There Are Even More Patriotic People Than Us.' However, Facts Always Fail to Prove That This Ideal is Absolutely True. Although Everyone's Circumstances Are Different, Everyone Has Their Own Patriotic Claims and National Salvation Actions, We Can't Find One or Two Effective and Obvious Facts. Take the 'National Product Movement' As an Example, We Are Convinced That National Products Can Fundamentally Save the Country, But How Much Effect Has It Had? Alas, It's a Pity to Say. Originally, The Enemy Who is Seizing Our Land, Infringing Upon Our Sovereignty, Raping Our People, and Cutting Off Our Livelihood Used Economic Policies to Invade and Exploit Us in Addition to Military Policies. His Merchants Are Mostly Military Spies, and His Soldiers Are Also Business Advisors. Their Military Policies Against Us Have Long Been Clearly Displayed Before Our Eyes, but Perhaps You Don't Fully Understand Their Economic Policies Actively Being Carried Out in Secret. Economic Policy is to Expand Rich Resources. They Don't Care About Three Times Seven Equals Twenty-One. As Long as There is a Place Where They Can Make Profits and Obtain Money, They Will Do Their Best to Operate. If They Can Sweep All the Money of Our Country's People in One Go, Then They Will Definitely Use Cannon Bombs and Explosions of Military Policies to Deal With Us Again. Therefore, They First Investigate Our People's Hobbies and Habits Clearly, and Aim at the Target to Manufacture All Kinds of Items That Our People Welcome, and Transport Them for Sale. Sure Enough, As They Expected, One Ship is Sold Out After One Ship is Transported, and Ten Ships Are Sold Out After Ten Ships Are Transported, Even Hundreds and Thousands of Ships, Coming in an Endless Stream and Selling Out Completely. Therefore, Last Year, The Value of Goods Imported Into Our Country Was As High As 120 Million Yuan. Alas, Our Fathers, Brothers, and Sisters, Aren't These 120 Million Good Foreign Dollars Awarded to Them by Our Chinese Citizens? If We Comprehensively Calculate the National Population and 120 Million Yuan, That is, Each of Us Will Lose 200 Yuan. If Everyone Buys National Products and Uses National Loans, Won't These 120 Million Yuan Still Flow Within the Country? If This Compatriot Spends It, That Compatriot Will Receive It Back. No Matter What, There Is Always Hope of Returning It to the Country. Since These 120 Million Yuan Have Left the Country, There Is No Need to Wait in Vain. Last Year Has Passed, and We Still Have to Cheer Up This Year, Make a Decision, and Only Then Can We Save Our Country. In Short, in One Sentence, Please, From Today's Bad Day of 'January 28th', All Items That You Wear, Use, Eat, and Use Every Day Should Be Purchased From National Products as Much as Possible. Also, Encourage All Relatives and Friends to Buy National Products. Cheap National Products Are a Minor Matter. Poverty, Exhaustion of Wealth, National Destruction, and Death Are a Major Matter. This Is the Easiest Thing to Do. This is the Thing That Matters Most to the Future of the Family and the Country. Everyone, Take This Opportunity to Make a Decision."

[Expressing Grief in the Declaration]:

The Association Specially Issued the Following Mourning Declaration Yesterday to Commemorate the Second Anniversary of January 28th: Following the Destruction of International Conventions on September 18, 1931 (September 18th Incident) and the Creation of an Excuse for Armed Invasion of Our Three Northeastern Provinces, the Japanese Used Airplanes and Cannons to Disrupt Shanghai at 11:00 PM on January 28th (January 28th Incident) of the Following Year, Namely Today Two Years Ago, After Our Shanghai Mayor Wu Guonian Took Into Account the Safety of Lives and Property in Chinese and Foreign Ports and Endured Humiliation to Accept the Four Unreasonable Demands of the Japanese. After the Japanese Consul Expressed Satisfaction to the Consuls of Various Countries, He Suddenly Used Airplanes and Cannons to Disrupt Shanghai, Using the Public Concession as a Military Base, Destroying Its Historical Neutrality, and Invading Zhabei, Destroying Almost All the Prosperity of Zhabeiwan Wusong, Etc. To This Day, It Is Still in Ruins and Debris. All Our Nationals Should Be Ashamed of This and Snow It Off. After September 18th, the Lost Land of the Eastern Provinces Has Not Been Recovered, the Central Government Still Has a Declaration of Sending Troops and Planning, and Important People Still Have a Vow to Command the Army North, But the Fact of Sincere Unity Still Has a Fleeting Appearance. After January 28th, There Was the Battle of Liu Han in Shandong, the Dispute Between Uncles and Nephews in Sichuan, and the Fight Between the Two Chens in Guangdong. Those Who Have No National Concept Took the Opportunity of the Northern Resistance Against Japan to Indulge in the Massacre of Huang Chao and Zhang Xianzhong. The Cadres of the Party Also Divided Their Ways, Still Using the Name of Resisting Insults From Abroad to Make Trouble on the Walls. Some Even Did Not Hesitate to Use the Anti-Japanese Fame of the 19th Route Army in Shanghai to Impulsively Change the Yuan Dynasty. Although It Was Only a Few People Who Had No Regard for the Interests of the Country and the People Who Intended to Harm Others for Their Own Benefit, It Was Actually Because the Power of the Party's Centralized Control Was Not Prepared. If This Is Not Planned to Determine a National Affair, It Is Still Not Easy to Secure It. How Can We Repel Foreign Aggressors? Although It Is Subjective to See What Is First and What Is Later in Securing the Interior and Repelling Foreign Aggressors, the Centralized Control of the Country Is Strong, and Repelling Foreign Aggressors Is Securing the Interior. All Our Nationals Can Deeply Understand This Meaning, But Now That This Condition Is Not Prepared Is the Most Painful. Fortunately, the Fourth Plenary Session of the Fourth Congress Has Been Opened, and Centralized Control Is Promising. Looking Back At the Decline of Shanghai's Commerce Due to the Decline of the Inland Rural Areas, the Destruction of January 28th Is Even More Declining. Those Who Exhaust the Ponds to Fish and Burn the Forests to Shield, and Those Who Extend Their Length to Exploit and Gather Can Only Cause Collapses to Occur One After Another and Unemployment to Increase Sharply. Even the Most Busy Nanjing Road, The Shops Are Also Seven Or Zero, Unable to Pay the Huge Rent. The Landlord Sues for Sealing Up the Shop, But the Court, Which Is Deeply Aware of the Social and Economic Situation, Advises Them to Settle. This Association Has Detailed Information on the Cost of Living Index. The Prices of Shanghai's Four Items Are All Falling With the Economic Situation of the Inland and the World. The Rent Item Has Been Increasing Since January 28th. This Is Why the Houses With Equal Monopoly Nature Can Take Advantage of the Situation and Hardly Change Their Rent Amount Due to the Relationship Between Supply and Demand. The Husband Returns Rice to Live in, Which Is Related to the People's Food, and the Official Office Will Ban It to Protect the People's Livelihood. Is It Not Harmful to the People's Livelihood to Return the House to Live in, Which Is Related to the People's Livelihood for the People Who Can Live in a Good Business? We Hope That the Official Office Will Ban It, and the Best Method Is to Levy House Donations on Empty Houses, One Is to Increase Tax Revenue, and the Other Is to Promote it. The Principles of Law and Human Feelings Are All Understandable, Which Is Not a Matter of Preparation With One Move and Several Goodness. On the Day When This Association Was on the Verge of Collapse in Shanghai, In View of the Painful Events of January 28th, It Zheng Told A Group of Exploiters and Gatherers That Shanghai's Economic Lifeline Is Prosperous in the Prosperity of the Inland and the Balance of Commerce. Today, The Inland is Declining, and the Annual Trade Surplus is Huge. In Addition, The Increase in Silver Use in the United States and the Increase in Silver Prices Have Caused the East Exchange to Shrink Sharply. In the Future, There Must Be Two Major Trends: (1) Outflow of Silver and Goods; (2) Foreign Dumping. As A Result of the Outflow of Silver and Goods, Shanghai's Chips Must Be Deficient, and A Tragic Fall in House Prices Can Be Expected. Foreign Goods Dumping, National Goods Commerce, It Is Even More Difficult to Stand. Clearing Up Bankruptcies Must Follow. Only Those Who Hold the Economic Function in Shanghai and Have Foresight Can Jointly Seek to Save It. The Rent Reduction Movement is Just a Reflection of Economic Decline. If the Government Does Not Provide Assistance, the Group Will Seek Survival, Then Shanghai's Destruction Is Not Far Away. It Is Not Only a Wei Great Building That Can Show Its Greatness. If You Do Not Plan Now and Die Together, Even There Are the Paramount, the Grand Light, and the Yangtze Hotel, Etc., It Is Not a Place for Exploiters to Gather." I Hereby Declare That All Are Publicly Appraised.

Statistical Analysis of Losses on Both Sides of the "January 28th" Anti-Japanese Memorial:

A Total of 9,210,000 National Currencies Were Lost.

Today is the Second Anniversary of the Songhu Anti-Japanese War. At the Time of the Bloody Battle Between the Two Sides, The Two-Way Administration Was the First to Bear the Brunt, Suffering an Unprecedented Disaster, With a Total Loss of 9,210,000 National Currencies. Zhang Qun Came to Shanghai Yesterday Morning and Talked About the Fact That the Reform of the Provincial System Is Underway. Chairman Chiang Will Go to Gan Within Days. There Is No Room for Reorganization of the 19th Route Army.

Zhang Qun, Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, Came to Shanghai by Night Train From Beijing at 7:30 Yesterday Morning After Attending the Fourth Plenary Session in Beijing. He Returned to Albert's Residence to Rest. At About 9 O'Clock, Chen Yi, the New Chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government, Visited to Discuss Various Issues Concerning the Aftermath of the Fujian Province and Had a Pleasant Conversation for Two Hours. Mr. Zhang Then Received Reporters From Various Newspapers and Scheduled to Stay in Shanghai for Two Days Before Returning to E. The Talks of Mr. Zhang Are Recorded Separately as Follows:

Reform of the Provincial System:

Mr. Zhang First Said That the Proposal on Reforming the Provincial System Was Jointly Proposed by Huang Shaoxiong, Minister of Internal Affairs, and Himself, But It Was Only Based on the Decisions of the Three Plenary Sessions and Added Organizational Opinions. After Being Passed by the General Assembly, It Was Submitted to the Central Political Conference to Draft the Organizational Law, Which Will Be Implemented on A Regular Basis. As for the Content of the Organization, There Were About Two Opinions Discussed At That Time: (1) Those Who Advocated That the Provincial Governor Should Have a Deputy Provincial Governor and Those Who Advocated That There Was No Need to Have A Deputy Provincial Governor; (2) The Departments Under the Provincial Government Still Used the Name of the Department, and Some Advocated That the Names of the Departments Such As Education and Construction Still Use the Name of the Department, While Others Such as Civil Affairs and Finance Were Changed to Departments. There Was Still No Body Decision, and It Was Also Submitted to the Central Political Conference for Detailed Discussion.

The End of the Rebellion:

The Issue of the Reorganization of the 19th Route Army Was Not Mentioned in the Plenary Session. Because the Army Has Suffered Heavy Casualties Since the Battles of Yanping Shuikou Gutian and Other Battles and Has Become Unformed, The Number of Those Who Survive Now Is Only A Few Thousand, With No Room for Reorganization. There Are Rumors That the Army Will Be Reorganized and Reorganized Under the Command of Dai Ji, Etc. Apart From the News in the Newspapers, I Have Not Heard of It. As for the Saying That the Southwest Asked the Central Government to Retain the Name of the 19th Route Army, It Is Not a Fact. The Central Army's Anti-Rebellion Military Affairs Can Be Completely Resolved, And the Southwest Authorities Have Not Made Such A Request to the Central Government. Chen Jitang Appointed Li Yangjing and Huang Renhuan As the Commanders and Deputy Commanders of the Guangdong-Fujian Border Defense, Which Was Approved by Chairman Chiang Before This Appointment. The Purpose Is to Block the Defeated Army.

The Recent Situation of E Government:

Regarding the Recent Situation in E Province, According to Mr. Zhang, The Expenses in E Province Are Very Difficult. However, In the Past Year, Regular Political Expenses Can Still Be Met With Difficulty. However, Because the Provincial Expenses Were Tight in the Past, All Facilities Had No Development, Especially the Education Expenses, Which Must Be Expanded. Therefore, It Has Been Decided That the 200,000 Yuan in Monthly Subsidies From the Central Government Should Be Used As Education Expenses. A Committee for the Safekeeping of Education Expenses Will Be Established to Manage and Distribute It Independently. It Has Now Been Submitted to the Central Government for Approval and Has Requested That the National Tax of E Province Be Directly Allocated to Avoid the Procedures of Applying to the Ministry of Finance. The Aftermath of Recovering the Bandit Areas Requires A Lot of Money, Which Has Been Planned by the Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression, So There Is No Need for E Province to Raise Money by Itself.

The Bandits in E Province Have Been Eliminated:

Mr. Zhang Also Said That Regarding the Military Affairs of Suppressing Bandits in E Province, In the Eastern Part of E Province, There Were Thousands of Bandits From Ye Jinbo. Since the Painful Suppression, There Are Only 300 People Left, Which Is Not Difficult to Completely Eliminate. The Bandit Units in the Western Part of E Province Have Also Been Defeated and Eliminated One After Another. As for Other Scattered Bandits, They Are Now Actively Being Eliminated. The Localities of the Whole Province Are Quite Safe and Have Not Changed At All.

Mr. Zhang Finally Said That After the Fourth Plenary Session, There Was Absolutely No Change in the Heads of Various Yuan Departments. The Rumors Outside Were Probably Created by Some Intentions. As for the Issue of Zhang Xueliang's Whereabouts, The Central Government Is Still Considering It and Has Not Made A Decision. I Will Stay in Shanghai for Two Days and Then Return to E. Chairman Chiang Is Still Staying in Beijing and Will Go to Gan Within Days, With No Need to Go to Fujian Again.

Chen Yi, Chairman of Fujian, Will Board the Ship Tonight and Leave Shanghai for Fujian Tomorrow Morning.

Chen Yi, the New Chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government, Was Ordered to Go to Fujian to Take Up His New Post. Petition to Preserve Water Conservancy by the People of Eight Townships in Ningbo 101

The Donglongtan Weir water inlet in Fenghua County has always been the lifeline of the farmland in eight townships, including Longxi, Daqiao, and Minghua. It is also the source of drinking water for most of the residents in the county, making it extremely important. It irrigates over 30,000 acres of farmland, making it the fertile fields of Fenghua County. Currently, the Fenghai Highway is being constructed, and to save on bridge construction costs, the roadbed will block the weir water. Moreover, without considering the elevation, the waterway is being altered. This has caused great alarm among the people of the eight townships, who have negotiated with the road construction site. Although Director Liu has agreed to add concrete culverts, it will not actually help. Therefore, the heads of the eight townships have elected representatives, including Zhang Zongming, the head of Minghua Township, Fang Xiang Sheng, the head of Daqiao Town, and Wang Yeguo, the head of Longxi Township. They have jointly submitted a petition based on two points: (1) The county's streams are full of sand and gravel, and the county often experiences heavy rain. The rapid currents and sand accumulation make it impossible for the stream water to enter the fields through the concrete culverts. (2) After heavy rains, sand and gravel flow downstream, turning today's deep pools into sand piles tomorrow. If concrete culverts are built, it will be difficult to adjust the elevation. If the sand piles are higher than the culverts, how can the stream water enter the fields through the culverts? (The original petition is long and not recorded here.) They are petitioning the Construction Department and Highway Bureau of the Zhejiang Provincial Government. The people of the townships believe that this matter concerns their vital interests and will not stop until their requests to maintain the original river and build a separate oblique bridge are granted.

Changshu Ice Thaws and Transportation Resumes 103

Due to the severe cold weather in the past few days, the rivers in various places froze. The steamers that relied on them for transportation were unable to pass on the 21st. As a result, mail was not delivered here, and the Shanghai newspapers did not arrive, causing a communication breakdown. With the year-end accounting period approaching, businesses were greatly affected. The Public Security Bureau made every effort to urge the steamer companies to break the ice and allow passage. As of the 24th, the Su-Chang and Kun-Chang routes have been cleared, and the weather has also warmed up slightly. The steamers immediately resumed operation, so the mail and newspapers of that day have arrived in Changshu.

[P Zhaoshangju Yu'an Ship in Xiamen Encountered Danger >

Loss of over 10,000 yuan... Can arrive in three days

The Zhaoshangju Nanyang liner Yu'an, which travels the Shanghai-Guangdong-Xiamen route, was carrying goods back to Shanghai this time when its machinery was damaged and its axle broke while traveling in the waters off Xiamen. The ship remained on the sea awaiting rescue. Yesterday, the bureau urgently dispatched Jiahe to tow it. It is estimated that it can return to Shanghai within three days. The losses are quite large. The situation is detailed as follows: The Yu'an, which encountered danger at sea, was leased by the Zhaoshangju from the Yu'an Shipping Company and assigned to the Nanhua route. The hull of the ship is very strong. This time, it carried goods from Guangdong back to Shanghai. It first arrived in Xiamen to load more goods. On the 24th, it departed from Xiamen. Unexpectedly, while traveling in the waters off Xiamen, between Xiamen and Fuzhou, at night, the ship's axle suddenly broke and the machinery was completely destroyed. The ship could not move. There was nothing to be done on the spot. It had to anchor in the sea area and send a telegram to Shanghai for help, so that it could be towed to the nearest coast for repair to avoid the danger of wind and waves.

Urgent Telegram for Assistance The owner of the Yu'an Ship urgently sent a wireless telegram to Shanghai to report the incident, requesting the Shanghai General Bureau to quickly send a tugboat to rescue it and tow the Yu'an to the nearest coast for repair. After receiving the report, the bureau immediately informed Zhao Yuntai, the owner of the Yu'an Company, to discuss the procedures for dispatching a tugboat for rescue. After a night of discussion, a decision was finally made yesterday afternoon.

Jiahe Rescues The Yu'an has been without its axle since the night of the 24th, which is now three days. If a large tugboat is hired from Shanghai to rescue it, it will take at least another three days. The wind and waves at sea are unpredictable, so it is difficult to delay further. Therefore, as a result of the discussion, it was decided to telegraph the Jiahe ship in Fuzhou to go to that location as soon as possible and tow the Yu'an to Shanghai for major repairs. This telegram has been sent to the two ships yesterday afternoon. The Jiahe ship can arrive that night. It will also transport food to the Yu'an to provide assistance.

Amount of Loss The reporter met Zhao Yuntai, who said that the loss of the Yu'an's axle and damaged machinery, together with the dispatch of tugboats and round-trip telegrams, would cost at least 10,000 yuan. The Yu'an has never had an accident since it was leased by the Zhaoshangju. This time, the machinery and axle must be completely replaced when it arrives in Shanghai. It is expected to arrive in Shanghai within three days.

Rui Gongxia Invents Domestic "Las Powder" 107

There are many nail factories in Shanghai, and the soap powder used for drawing lead wire is all imported. According to the customs import table, the amount is huge, and the outflow of money is countless. Rui Gongxia, a native of Ningbo, studied chemical engineering in Germany to resist foreign countries and recover rights and interests. After returning to China in August of last year, he raised funds to establish Zhenya Chemical Industry Co., Ltd. He also devoted himself to research and invented domestic lead wire drawing soap powder, named domestic "Las Powder". It has now been successfully launched. The powder is better than imported products and the price is three times cheaper. It is truly a new undertaking in the national goods year.

More Than 5,000 Yuan of Stolen Goods Recovered in Hongtai Pawnshop Robbery Case 108

Police Still Capturing Major Thieves

Yesterday morning, the Hongtai pawnshop at 624 Changchun Lane, Tangshan Road, Hongkou, was broken into by several thieves who dug through the wall and stole all the gold jewelry, clothing, and silver dollars, worth over 10,000 yuan, before fleeing. The pawnshop manager, Jin Maoqin, reported the case to the police and requested an investigation. Around 7:30 p.m. the day before yesterday, the Hua detectives Ye Chuanxi and Liu Qingsheng from the General Patrol House learned that the gang was dividing the loot at 6 Huashou Lane, Zhoushan Road. They immediately coordinated with Chinese and foreign detectives to rush to arrest them, but the thieves had already fled after hearing the news. Only an old woman, Cao Zhangshi, was arrested. Seven bullets, several iron tools used for digging through the door, and original stolen clothes and jewelry worth over 5,000 yuan were found in the house. They were all taken back to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Criminal Court No. 1 of the First Special Court. The police lawyer, Li Zhishan, stated that the police were conducting a thorough investigation and arresting major thieves, so he requested a postponement of the trial. Qian Hongye, the head of the Criminal Court, approved the request and ordered Cao Zhangshi to be detained for a further review.

Three Teachers from the Sino-French School Receive Gold Medals 109

Serving for Twenty-Five Years

The Sino-French School in Shanghai's Baxianqiao has been established for nearly fifty years, producing numerous talents and achieving outstanding results, and has been trusted by society. The Fifth Branch of the Second Municipal Federation Requests Prohibition of Dog Racing and Jai Alai 110

Letter Sent to Taxpayers' Association and Other Organizations Yesterday

The Fifth District Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District Citizens' Federation in Tangjiawan, French Concession, sent letters to the French Concession Chinese Ratepayers' Association and the Municipal Federation regarding the issue of dog racing and jai alai, requesting the French authorities to strictly prohibit them. The original letter is recorded below: "Dear Sirs, the matter of requesting the prohibition of dog racing and jai alai has been repeatedly proposed by members of our association. Now, in accordance with the decision of the fifteenth executive committee meeting of our association, we send a letter requesting your association to send a letter to the French Municipal Council and submit it to the French Consul General, Mr. Meriel, for strict prohibition. We also send a letter to the Chinese Directors, making suggestions to the French Municipal Council, because dog racing and jai alai are using entertainment as a pretext to lead the public into gambling. Gambling is a criminal act, and the provisions of Articles 278 to 281 of our country's criminal law are very clear and should be strictly prohibited, but they are allowed to be open, which is especially harmful to society. Moreover, dog racing has long been strictly prohibited in the Public Concession, but in the French Concession, not only is there no clear prohibition, but it is openly allowed, which is deeply bewildering. The prosperity of the people's livelihood is affected by the safety and stability of the region. Those in power should guide the people to diligence and thrift, not tempt them to take risks and gamble. There is no difference in this principle in ancient and modern times, at home and abroad. Shanghai is the center of factories in the country, and the majority of the people are laborers. In recent years, due to the economic downturn, various industries have declined, and the hardships of life are more severe than in other places. Even without unexpected consumption, they are already in a precarious situation. The jai alai and dog racing exploit the people's weak psychology, tempting them with the prospect of a hundred or a thousandfold return. All eyes are focused on this great opportunity. Those who enter the field appreciate the low cost and admire the quick way to get rich. Even women and children, peddlers and coolies, even those who cannot afford to eat, want to do everything possible to scrape together their hard-earned money in order to try their luck. The harm is extremely serious. In recent years, with the special permission of the French authorities as protection, the monthly income of these two places is no less than millions of dollars. This is all the money that the lower and middle classes need to maintain their lives. In a shift, they are cleverly and forcibly seized and fall into the hands of others. If this exploitation continues, the lives of the people will become more difficult, and chaos will arise. The relationship to local security is not insignificant. Moreover, knowing that success is difficult, they have no choice but to drink poison and resign themselves to their fate. Even if they fail in one strike, the funds are squandered, and they still hope to recover their losses elsewhere. Therefore, once a commoner enters the shell, they will never be able to extricate themselves for the rest of their lives. And because of this, there are frequent reports of people who are bankrupt and take risks. There have also been many cases of business embezzlement and fraudulent behavior due to gambling debts. Its poison is comparable to morphine. Although a small portion of the income is used to subsidize one or two charitable causes, weighing the pros and cons, the gains do not compensate for the losses. We hope that you will submit a request for a limited time to prohibit it, so as to show the determination to eradicate evil, and it will also be helpful to refresh politics. Hundreds of millions of people in Shanghai will be truly blessed."

A Young Traveler Commits Suicide by Taking Poison in the Dongya Hotel 111

In the Dongya Hotel on Nanjing Road, a young man wearing a suit and about 20 years old checked in the afternoon before yesterday. The hotel cashier led him to room 447 on the fourth floor. The young man wrote his surname as Wei, his name as Wufei, from Beiping, a student, and paid the room fee of three yuan on the spot. He closed the door and went to sleep in the evening. Until 9:00 a.m. yesterday, he had not yet gotten up. The tea server went to knock on the door to ask if the room was still needed. Unexpectedly, there was no response for a long time, which aroused suspicion. He quickly found a way to open the door and enter the room. He saw that the young man's face was pale and his breath was weak. He had been unconscious for a long time. The tea server and others quickly reported to the cashier, who in turn reported to the Old Gate Police Station. They rushed to send an ambulance to the Renji Hospital for treatment. Unfortunately, he had taken too much poison and died on the way. The body was transferred to the autopsy office to report to the court for inspection. An investigation was also launched to identify the corpse.

Judge to Visit the Scene of the Woman Who Fell to Her Death from a Brothel 112

Meeting on Improvement of Songhu Branch Line by the Two-Road Transportation Office

Concrete Measures Have Been Decided 114

The Songhu Branch Line of the Jinghu Railway is the first railway line created in China and has a long history in the history of Chinese railways. In addition, with the recent relocation of the Shanghai Municipal Government to the city center, the importance of the line has increased. Therefore, its business must be improved to adapt to the needs of the times, which is an urgent task. The Transportation Office convened a discussion meeting on the improvement of the branch line at 2:30 p.m. on the 25th of this month, attended by Deputy Director Yuan, Deputy Director Xie, Chief Mao of the General Affairs Section, Chief Wang of the Transportation Section, Chief Wang of the Su-Song Section of the Jinghu Line, Chief Tang of the Resident Office, and Clerk Zou, who was temporarily transferred to manage the reorganization of the Songhu Branch Line. It was divided into personnel, material, business, and transportation aspects for detailed discussion, in order to gather ideas and plan improvement methods. Most of the personnel summoned to attend had fully prepared proposals, totaling thirteen items, which were discussed separately. Concrete measures have been decided and will be announced after being organized.

Police Officer's Wife Dies of Coal Poisoning 116

Ma Gao, a 21-year-old woman from Xuzhou, was the wife of Ma Juli, who was a Chinese patrol officer No. 136 in the Tilanqiao Prison. They had been married for five years and had a good relationship. Ms. Ma gave birth to a daughter two weeks ago and was weak as a result. She had also been feeling headaches recently, so she was bedridden during the day. The day before yesterday, Ma, seeing that his wife was weak due to the cold weather, prepared a coal stove for her and placed it in her bedroom. At about 2:00 p.m., Ms. Ma suddenly became faint. Ma was extremely alarmed and sent his wife to Guangren Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective and she died. The hospital reported to the Huishan Police Station, which ordered investigator Shen Binkui to investigate. The body was taken to the Feilun Road Autopsy Office. Yesterday morning, Zhang Junqing, a prosecutor from the First Special District Local Court, together with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Gong Wang Zuyi, arrived at the office to examine the body. According to the statement of the deceased's husband, Ma Juli, 23 years old, "My bedroom is behind the living room. I prepared a coal stove that day and initially placed it in the room. Later, because my wife walked to the living room for lunch, I moved the coal stove out to keep her warm. After she sat there for about an hour, she went back to the room to sleep. She had no other illnesses on weekdays, only headaches after giving birth." Mr. Zhang obtained the statement and ordered that the deceased, Ma Gao, female, died of coal poisoning. The body was handed over to her husband, Ma Juli, to claim and bury.

Found in Wu Naiquan's House

Gao Qingtang, Shen Yinzhang, Li Erbao, and Zhu Naiquan from Yangzhou colluded to deceive Wang Wu, a young woman from Jiaxing, 18 years old, and her younger sister, Wu Qin'e, 16 years old, to come to Shanghai between December 29th and stayed in a hotel, intending to sell Qin'e. On the 10th of the month, Wang Zhusheng, a Chinese detective from the Hongkou Police Station, and Detective Zhang Desheng, learned of the matter and secretly went to Zhejiang Hotel on Hankou Road, 700 Edward Road, and 837 Tiantong Road to arrest Gao and the other three and rescue Wang Wu. After arriving in Shanghai, they first stayed at the Wenminxing Inn on Edward Road. That night, Gao tried to force himself on Wu Qin'e but failed and tried to sell her. The next day, Gao returned to his hometown and invited his neighbor, Li Erbao, the defendant, to come to Shanghai and moved into the Yuanyuan Inn at 223 Fuzhou Road. Li took Qin'e to a relative of his named Yang on Baker Road and explained the intention. Yang saw that the matter was inappropriate and immediately refused. Later, a person named Zhang Lianqing took Qin'e to the defendant Zhu Naiquan at 700 Edward Road, wanting to buy her for 300 yuan. It was found that Yang was a pimp in a low-class brothel, and he intended to pay 250 yuan for Qin'e because she was petite and exquisite. However, he had no money and left her there temporarily. The cheongsam that Qin'e is wearing is the old one worn by his 17-year-old daughter. The clothes are the symbol of a prostitute, and it is possible that she has already engaged in prostitution. Judge Liu then questioned each of the defendants and ordered them to be detained separately pending a further hearing.

Reading Q&A

The Fundamental Problem of Reading 129

(1) High ambitions in reading and no standards for choosing subjects to study ...... I am a reader of your library, and thanks to your library, I have developed my reading habit. In the beginning, it was nothing more than aimless browsing, but because I love books like my life, I almost want to read the best books in the world before I am satisfied; but due to the pressure of the environment, I have to be greatly disappointed. ... (Letter from Zhang Tingshan)

...... After reading the "Reading Problems" on the 13th and 14th of this month, I am very depressed because I am a person (lost in the sea of ​​learning). I like to study all kinds of subjects and I am interested in them; I like to study social sciences, because it can tell me the relationship between people, and I also love natural sciences, because it can explain natural phenomena. Therefore, I am just like Mencius said, "I want both bear's paws and fish", but from the gentlemen's answers, I know that "you can't have both." But which one to give up and which one to take, I really don't have the courage to decide. I am like being trapped in the abyss of a love triangle. I love the two girls equally. How can I weigh them and specialize in one subject? But, you want me to decide on a subject, and in fact, you can only let me study one subject, so I will reluctantly give up natural science and study social science ...... (Letter from Dong Yuan)

Reading the above two letters reminds us of what the Japanese writer Natsume Kinnosuke said. He said··

"When you are young and strong, before you can make some contributions to your own specialized studies, you think that you must be proficient in all aspects, and you must read through thousands of years of books in ancient and modern times. If you have to do this, then you will be old and you will never have a period of proficiency in all aspects. People like me, I really can't say that I am proficient in the entire English study. Probably in another two or thirty years, I will still be unable to understand it." ..." (See Yu Dafu's Literature People's slight reference)

Natsume Kinnosuke's words are indeed reading experience; and we have also solemnly advised readers on "several issues about choosing subjects"·· I hope they do not choose too many subjects, "Because when ambitions are too big, disappointments will definitely increase. As a result, you will become self-abandoning and fail to do anything. Therefore, the most fearful thing for us beginners is to sing high-sounding but impractical tunes." (Mr. Yu Dafu's words)

Therefore, from a practical point of view, from the point of view of reading efficiency, it is impossible to have extravagant expectations when reading at the beginning. But from these two letters, we can also see: the strong desire for knowledge and the huge ambitions of reading in every young person; they want to read every book and want to understand every event and every phenomenon in the universe. Therefore, as Dong Yuan's letter said, beginners have no love or hate for various subjects and treat them equally. This is an unstoppable hope, although it will be subject to practical obstacles, but it cannot be eliminated after all. Therefore, we know that it is proper and necessary to ask beginners to narrow the scope of research; but for this reason, we ask them to choose subjects to study and tell them that too much desire for knowledge will lead to failure. Not only will it reduce their interest in research, but their choice of subjects will also be standardless, because there is no special reason for this choice.

Therefore, we do not want beginners to immediately study by subject, but advocate that they first read some basic and common books. (Conclusions and measures will be announced on the 30th)

By mail: Mr. Zhang Xianzong and Zhu Jiaming, please send the most recent contact address to the library for reply.

Education News

Other Cities 130

The Ministry of Education Organizes the Northeast Youth Education Relief Office

On the 26th, the Ministry of Education announced the organizational regulations of the Northeast Youth Education Relief Office, consisting of thirteen articles as follows:

Article 1: In order to handle the education relief affairs of Northeast youth, the Ministry of Education shall establish the Northeast Youth Education Relief Office (hereinafter referred to as the Office) in accordance with Article 2 of the Provisional Relief Measures for Northeast Hardworking Students. Article 2: The Office shall be located in Nanjing, and branch offices shall be established at appropriate locations in North China. Article 3: The Office shall have one director, who shall be supervised by the Ministry of Education and shall direct and manage the affairs of the entire Office. The Office shall have one deputy director, who shall assist the director in handling various affairs. The director and deputy director mentioned in the preceding paragraph shall be appointed by the Ministry of Education. Article 4: The Office shall temporarily establish the following two groups: (1) Group 1 shall handle documents, general affairs, accounting, statistics, and all matters not belonging to Group 2; (2) Group 2 shall handle various matters relating to investigation and supervision. Article 5: Each group shall have one group leader to handle the affairs of the group. The Office shall have several staff members, clerks, and employees to perform their duties. They shall be appointed by the director and reported to the Ministry for record. Article 6: The Office shall have one secretary to handle and review important documents. The secretary shall be appointed by the director and reported to the Ministry for record. Article 7: The Office shall establish a review committee to review the qualifications of students requesting subsidies, and it may apply to the Ministry of Education for approval to establish other committees as needed to handle examinations or other special affairs. The organizational methods of the above-mentioned committees shall be drafted by the Office and submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval and implementation. Article 8: The Office may request the Ministry of Education to assign Ministry staff members or order its affiliated agencies to assist as necessary for handling affairs. Article 9: The director and deputy director of the Office shall inspect the studies of the subsidized students at any time and provide necessary guidance in their lives. Article 10: The Office shall report its work status and revenue and expenditure to the Ministry of Education on a monthly basis and make public announcements as necessary. Article 11: The Office shall establish an office affairs meeting to promote various tasks. The rules shall be determined separately. Article 12: The detailed rules for handling various affairs of the Office shall be determined separately. Article 13: These Regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Detailed Record of the Second Day of the Annual Meeting of the Chinese Education Association 131

Morning Meeting

The second annual meeting of the Chinese Education Association was held on the morning of the 25th at the Central University South Gaoyuan, presided over by Chen Jiantiao. The news was reported yesterday. The following resolutions were made on this day in addition to reading the papers: (1) A proposal to submit the new standards for primary and secondary school courses promulgated by the Ministry for research (with a proposal to organize a committee to conduct group research and report the results at the next annual meeting). It was resolved to designate several primary and secondary schools and recommend several members to jointly organize a committee to study the new curriculum standards for primary and secondary schools and submit a report on the research results at the next annual meeting. (2) A temporary motion that the central government's education funds should account for a certain percentage of the total national revenue and that local education funds should account for a certain percentage of the total local revenue and that the government should be requested to stipulate this. It was resolved that the board of directors would appoint a committee to collect materials on the percentage of education funds in various countries and the percentage of education funds in various provinces in China, conduct research, report to the board of directors, and make suggestions to the government. (3) A motion that the current joint examination system should be discussed and resolved urgently. Members such as Shao Shuangqiu and Ma Ketan expressed their opinions. Wu Yan reported the results of the Ministry of Education's investigation of education departments in various provinces and the general opinions other than administrative ones. They felt that the joint examination for primary schools was difficult and that the joint examination for middle schools was necessary, but the method needed to be changed. The Ministry of Education has now temporarily exempted primary schools from the joint examination, and the method for the joint examination for middle schools has been revised and announced. Therefore, the joint examination system seems to be no longer a problem, only a research problem on the method (such as the necessary materials, subjects, and scoring and scoring methods for the joint examination). Huang Jianzhong said that he did not agree with the primary school joint examination system, but the middle school joint examination, especially the senior high school general course, made the level uniform, which facilitated further studies. He also cited the joint examination system in British middle schools for explanation. The chairman said that this case would be handed over to the board of directors to send personnel to jointly study with the Chinese Measurement and Examination Association so that there would be considerable results. The name does not necessarily have to be "Research on the Joint Examination System", but it can be a method of measuring students' grades, which will be determined by the two associations in the future. Everyone agreed. (4) How should the direction and curriculum of university education departments be stipulated? Because this case was already a central research question in yesterday's discussion topic, it was no longer discussed. (5) A proposal to organize a "National Spirit" teaching material committee to engage in research and collect national spirit teaching materials so that they can be incorporated into textbooks (with a proposal that the committee be organized by the association and work with the education departments of various universities to engage in research and editing so that they can be incorporated into Chinese language, history, and civics textbooks for primary and secondary schools in the future). It was resolved to hand it over to the board of directors for consideration.

Public Banquet Situation 132

After the discussion, it was already 12:30. The Central Political School, Central University, Jinling University, and Jinling Women's College of Arts and Sciences held a public banquet for the members at the Lao Wanquan Restaurant.

Afternoon Meeting 133

The meeting continued at 3:00 PM in the afternoon. Chairman Yang Lianggong first reported on the summary text of the "Plan for Rapid Success of Universal Education in China" sent by Tao Zhixing, which will be printed and sent later. He then reported that Li Zheng, president of Beijing Normal University, sent a telegram to congratulate the meeting and welcome the next annual meeting to be held at the school. Cheng Qibao, director of the Hubei Education Department, also sent a telegram to welcome the next annual meeting to be held in Hubei and promised to be responsible for accommodating the members. The discussion of association affairs then began. (1) A motion on the date and location of the next annual meeting of the association. Zhuang Zexuan said that the association's annual meeting only lasted for two days. In order to conduct more research, he suggested that the association and a university jointly organize a summer seminar during the annual meeting to concentrate on studying problems and give specialized lectures, imitating the methods of the Fujian Education Department. First, contact which university to jointly organize the summer seminar and then hold the meeting there. Yuan Dunli said that he was a professor at Beijing Normal University. Since President Li sent a congratulatory telegram, he could represent Beijing Normal University and was willing to jointly organize the seminar with the association. The members discussed the location problem and submitted five votes. As a result, Beijing (28 people raised their hands), Hangzhou (16), Wuxi (10), Lushan (7), and Qingdao (6). The majority advocated that Beijing be the first location and Hangzhou be the second location. The board of directors was asked to decide on one. Zheng Xiaocang advocated adding Wuxi to the board of directors. Zhuang Zeyi and Chen Jianxiao both advocated handing all five locations to the board of directors, writing down the number of people who voted, arranging the order, and letting the board of directors designate them. Everyone agreed. The annual meeting was scheduled to be held during the summer vacation next year. (2) A motion on the problem of the association's meeting place. The chairman reported that Director Tao Zhixing proposed two locations for the meeting place: (1) Wantuo Temple outside Heping Gate; (2) A village in the near suburbs outside Tongji Gate. Please choose one and run a practical experimental school here. Some members advocated building a meeting place, some advocated renting a house, some advocated jointly building with other societies, and some advocated running a practical experimental school. Zhuang Zexuan, Tong Runzhi, Zheng Xiaocang, Ou Yuanhuai, Zheng Tonghe, Ma Ketan, and others also expressed their opinions. After the chairman voted, it was unanimously decided that the association must have a meeting place. As for how to establish the meeting place, it was up to the board of directors to decide. Whether or not to attach a practical experimental school was handed over to the next annual meeting for discussion. (3) It was resolved in principle to raise funds to hire a special person, which was handed over to the board of directors. (4) A motion to increase group members and permanent members was passed, and it was agreed that those who paid 30 yuan at once (including a 5 yuan membership fee) would be permanent members, and those who paid 200 yuan or more at once or 50 yuan per year would be group members. After passing this motion, the articles of association had to be revised. The chairman appointed Liu Tingfang, Zhuang Zexuan, and Chen Lijiang to revise the articles of association in another room and continue the discussion. (5) The motion to compile the association's series of publications was passed. (6) The motion to establish a resident staff member for the association was resolved to be established by the board of directors when necessary. (7) It was proposed that the conference require the board of directors to continue to draft. (8) The motion to edit a catalog of books related to education by members of the association was handed over to the board of directors. (9) The board of directors was requested to continue to edit abstracts of educational books and newspapers and to review educational terms, which was passed.

Revision of Association Articles 134

(10) Revision of Association Articles Proposal: After discussion, it was decided to have Liu Tingfang report on the revision of the articles of association. After discussion, the following articles of the association were decided to be revised (articles not revised are not recorded): (1) Add Article 4 (The members of this association are divided into two types: individual members and group members). (2) Article 4 is changed to Article 5 (Anyone who has specialized research in education or has made contributions to education, introduced by two or more members of this association, and approved by the board of directors of this association, may become an individual member of this association). Add Article 6 (Any educational group or organization that sponsors the work of this association, proposed by two or more members of this association, and approved by the board of directors of this association, may be invited by letter to become a group member of this association). Article 5 is changed to Article 7 (Individual members pay an admission fee of five yuan upon joining the association and an annual fee of two yuan. In addition to the admission fee of five yuan, groups paying twenty-five yuan at one time may become permanent members and are exempt from the annual fee). Add Article 8 (Group members pay an admission fee of two hundred yuan or more upon joining the association and an annual fee of fifty yuan). Article 6 is changed to Article 9 (The association has a board of directors composed of individual members and representatives of group members (one person from each group). The board is composed of fifteen directors elected by the public to plan the association's activities. The term of office is one year, and they may be re-elected). Articles 7 to 13 below are changed to Articles 10 to 16 (three articles are added to the articles of association).

Following the vote, the majority advocated that the fifteen directors to be re-elected in this session should be chosen by drawing lots to serve one, two, or three-year terms, so that one-third of the directors would be re-elected in the next session. Subsequently, Zhang Boling delivered the closing speech, elaborating on the advantages and disadvantages of running education in China, future ideas for saving the country through education, and his personal hopes for the association. The meeting adjourned after 6 PM. In the evening, the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government hosted a public banquet for all members in the auditorium of the Ministry of Education.

Liu Tingfang, Zhuang Zexuan, Zheng Xigu, Zheng Xiaocang, Chen Lijiang, Yang Lianggong, Xu Keshi, Shao Shuangqiu, Chen Jianxiao, Chang Daozhi, Zhang Boling, Ou Yuanhuai, Tao Zhixing, Meng Xiancheng, and Du Zuozhou were elected as directors. Xie Xunchu, Ai Wei, Chen Qibao, Chen Heqin, and Guo Yicen were elected as alternate directors.

Jiangsu Provincial Military Instructors Conference 136

Military Education Must Be Increased in All Schools Above the High School Level

Students Who Fail Military Training Will Not Be Promoted or Graduate

Suggest Ministry of Education Revise Military Training Curriculum for Universities and Middle Schools

The Jiangsu Provincial National Training Committee, in order to rectify military training throughout the province, specially convened military instructors from various schools on the 25th and 26th of this month in Suzhou to discuss the essential issues of implementing military training. The details of the meeting are recorded as follows:

Attending Instructors: Military instructors from schools in various counties, including Huang Xianli (Suzhou Agricultural School), Chen Diping (Changzhou Middle School), Xu Wanlan (Nantong School), He Liangxin (Fisheries School), He Jisu (Nanjing Middle School), Zhao Zihe (Nanjing Middle School), Zhou Chaofan (Nanjing Middle School), Su Jun (Tongzhou Middle School), Wang Ke (Huaishi Normal School), Huang Jinwen (Rushi Normal School), Wang Yixuan (Soochow University), Tang Shiquan (Suzhou Middle School), Jiang Zhenlan (Xizhong Middle School), Xu Xienong (Shanghai Middle School), Liu Pingfan (Songzhong Middle School), Wang Weixian (Zhenshi Normal School), Tang Yuanli (Xijiao College), Zeng Weigong (Yizhong Middle School), He Zhihao, representative of the Training Headquarters, Huang Zigao, representative of the Provincial Department of Education, and Jiang Chuan, representative of the Security Office.

Glimpses of Proposals: The meeting opened at 9 AM on the morning of the first day, chaired by Hu Dun and recorded by Chen Shaokun. First, the chairman reported that the best results in the province were from Taicang Normal School and Suzhou Shizhong School, while Soochow University and Yangzhou were the worst. In the afternoon, proposals were discussed: (1) The proposal to set a three-week exercise period to allow students to experience military life was resolved to be postponed. (2) The proposal to standardize military training equipment was resolved to (A) submit to the General Training Headquarters a request to establish a factory for military training educational equipment to standardize teaching materials throughout the province, and (B) designate required teaching materials and equipment by this conference and order instructors from various schools to purchase them. (3) The current training grounds and fields are based on German training manuals, but each item should have specified instructions. It was resolved that the conference should submit a request to the General Training Headquarters and send a letter to military academies to issue reference books specifically for shooting instruction methods. (4) The proposal to establish school teams was resolved that military education must be increased in all schools above the high school level, and the right to manage and punish with military discipline should be drafted by this conference and submitted to the General Training Headquarters to consult with the Ministry of Education and instruct the provincial departments to forward it to various schools. (5) The proposal to strictly order schools to earnestly comply with the rule that students who fail military training should not be promoted or graduate was resolved to submit this case, based on Chiang Kai-shek's December 1, 22nd year Dongdai telegram, to the General Training Headquarters to consult with the Ministry of Education. (6) The proposal to increase the number of military training courses in high schools to include military management and academic assistance was resolved to submit a suggestion to the General Training Headquarters. (7) The proposal to improve the university military training curriculum was resolved to have each instructor submit a list of opinions within one month, collect them, and then suggest to the Ministry to revise the military training curriculum for universities and middle schools. (8) The proposal to find ways to subsidize military training equipment for private high schools and above was resolved to have the conference submit a request to the provincial government to allocate military training funds each year according to the school's expenses. (9) The proposal to delete the "three generations" column from the student survey form upon completion of military training was resolved to submit a revision request to the Ministry. (10) The proposal for military officers in various schools to promote military songs was resolved to request the Ministry to collect and compile student military songs. (11) The proposal to request schools to issue guns was resolved to submit a request to the Ministry of Military Affairs to approve the purchase of guns by schools that have implemented military training for practice. (12) The proposal to equip schools with military affairs was resolved to be retained. (13) The proposal to establish bugler units in each school was resolved to request the Department of Education to order schools to strictly implement bugle calls during holidays. If a bugler cannot be recruited, the instructor can recommend one. (14) The proposal to ban schools from privately hiring instructors was resolved to be retained.

International Conference on Educational Films 138

Our Country's Educational Film Association Has Sent Representatives

Conference Discussion Scope Announced

The International Educational Film Association, affiliated with the League of Nations, is scheduled to hold an international conference on educational films in Rome from April 4th to 7th this year, which was prepared last year. The Italian Embassy in China has received instructions from the government and sent a letter to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting it to forward it to relevant domestic agencies and individuals engaged in educational films to attend. The Italian government also approved a 70% reduction in train fares. The China Educational Film Association has requested Mr. Zhu Ying, Secretary of the Chinese Embassy in Italy, to attend. The scope of the conference's discussion has been defined and announced in three parts: (1) Teaching, (2) Education, and (3) Film and International Relations. Each part is further divided into plenary discussions and group committee discussions. The sources of materials collected include: (1) the results of research and investigation by various departments of the League of Nations Educational Film Association, (2) answers to various questions sent to relevant agencies and organizations, and (3) reports from groups or individuals and discussions on research on certain issues. In addition, reports from various countries on the implementation of educational films in their own countries. The first part on teaching is divided into four committees for discussion: (1) Methods of teaching films, (2) Films in school education, (3) Pedagogical films and child psychology, and (4) National and school films. The second part on education is divided into five committees: (1) Chronicle and verification films, (2) Health and preventive films, (3) Film and public education, (4) Film and social relief, and (5) National and international museums and proposals. The third part discusses film and international relations, divided into two committees: (1) Film and national life, and (2) International issues regarding the circulation of educational films.

Municipal Education Bureau Promulgates Measures to Supervise School Enrollment 147

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued instructions yesterday to municipal and registered private secondary schools, stating that school enrollment must go through entrance exams to assess whether students have the appropriate academic ability, which is extremely important. In order to prevent malpractices, schools must submit a report to the bureau in advance so that personnel can be sent to supervise the exams at the time. The bureau issued a notice to all schools for compliance in May of the 19th year of the Republic of China. However, with the passage of time, schools have often gone their own way in enrollment and entrance exams, failing to comply with the order to report. This is not appropriate. The bureau has now specifically revised the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's Provisional Measures for Supervising Secondary School Enrollment, which will be promulgated and implemented immediately. In addition to reporting to the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government for the record, all schools are ordered to comply with these measures for each enrollment and entrance exam. Do not violate this order. Attached is the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's Provisional Measures for Supervising Secondary School Enrollment: (1) All schools in this city (hereinafter referred to as "schools") must comply with these measures for each enrollment. (2) All schools must conduct entrance exams for each enrollment, regardless of new students or transfer students. During the exams, physical examinations, written tests, and oral tests must be conducted separately. (3) Each school's entrance exam is limited to a maximum of three times per session and may not be taken at any time. (4) Each school shall submit a completed enrollment report form prepared by the bureau ten days before the entrance exam. (5) Each school shall prepare its own entrance exam schedule, clearly stating the exam subjects and times, and submit it to the bureau at the same time as the enrollment report form. (6) The bureau may send personnel to supervise the entrance exams of each school on a temporary basis. (7) The bureau may randomly check and review the entrance exam papers of each school at any time. (8) Within ten days after the completion of all entrance exams, each school shall complete a student entrance exam score sheet and submit it to the bureau in accordance with the entrance exam process report form prepared by the bureau. (9) These measures may be amended at any time if there are any matters not covered. (10) These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Municipal Education Bureau Orders Municipal Elementary Schools to Report Monthly Expenses on Time 148

Starting from August of This Year

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued instructions yesterday to municipal elementary schools, stating that the budget for regular expenses for municipal elementary schools in the 22nd year of the Republic of China has not yet been approved. Therefore, starting from August, the monthly expenses will be temporarily issued and received in accordance with the old budget. Therefore, the monthly reports have been temporarily postponed. Now that the budget for regular expenses for municipal elementary schools this year has been approved, all the expenses that were short-issued each month starting from August have been fully reissued and received. The monthly expense calculation data for each school should be reported on time for review and transfer. In the future, monthly reports should still be submitted monthly to comply with the regulations. You are ordered to comply with and report without delay. This order.

President Sattiah of Yenching University Lectures on "Chinese University Students" 149

At the Invitation of the Rotary Club Yesterday

Dr. Sattiah, President of Yenching University in Beiping, is an American who grew up in China, knows Chinese psychology well, and speaks fluent Chinese. He can be called an American of China. He lectured at the Rotary Club yesterday on "Chinese University Students." He first outlined the employment problems of university students in various countries. Only 30% of university students in the United States can find jobs, and Europe is slightly the same. Due to the rapid increase in population in Japan, only 20% of university students can find jobs. India is also the same. However, most unemployed students are engaged in revolutionary activities. The current crisis in Chinese education is that it is not easy for ordinary university students to find jobs. Often what they learn is not what they use, and the government cannot accommodate them as much as possible. He hopes to remedy this. Sattiah's arguments were correct and well received by the audience.

Ministry of Education Orders Shanghai Night Schools to Stop Enrollment; Soochow Has Also Received Instructions 151

The Ministry of Education has ordered night schools run by various colleges and universities in Shanghai to stop enrolling new students and close in phases. Four schools, including Hujiang, Chih Tze, Politics and Law, and Business College, have received instructions, as reported previously. It is now learned that the night school of Soochow Law School has also received the same instructions. Therefore, the reason why the Ministry of Education wants to shut down night schools this time is not a matter of the quality of the schools themselves, but that the system of night schools is unsuitable. In particular, night school students have many inconveniences in terms of military training and self-study. Therefore, it is ordered that all night schools in Shanghai, regardless of their level, stop enrolling new students and close in phases. It is found that there are a total of five colleges and universities in Shanghai with night schools, including Soochow, Hujiang, Chih Tze, Politics and Law, and Business College. After receiving the instructions from the Ministry of Education, some immediately complied with the order and closed, such as Hujiang and Business College, and some closed in phases, such as Soochow, Chih Tze, and Politics and Law. As for the closing methods and how to close in phases, a certain gentleman from the Ministry of Education said that it depends on the situation of each school.

Those who are interested in studying should register and take the exam immediately. Qingru Primary School: Qingru Primary School, registered with the Municipal Education Bureau on Huacheng Road in the French Concession, has always had strict management and effective teaching methods. Starting this semester, it has added a Chinese and Western language night school, with internal divisions for Chinese, English, Japanese, French, Russian, German, commercial accounting, typing, mathematics, physics, and other subjects. The professors hired are all bachelors from domestic and foreign universities. It is reported that the school is scheduled to open on February 1st and classes will begin on the 3rd. Those who have gone to register and apply for the exam have been quite enthusiastic.

Lianyi Primary School: Lianyi Primary School, a private complete primary school registered with the Municipal Education Bureau in Lianyi Fang, Xiafei Road, French Concession, is scheduled to open on February 1st and will begin accepting registrations for male and female students from today, placing them in grades according to their level. It is reported that the school will expand its enrollment this year and also accept boarders.

Shanghai Girls' High School: Shanghai Girls' High School on Xieqiao Manufacturing Bureau Road in this city has long been approved and registered by the Municipal Education Bureau. The school board members, Lin Kanghou, Wu Tiecheng, Chu Minyi, Wu Xingya, Zhou Bangjun, Tao Baichuan, Pan Yangyao, and others, have provided much guidance to the school. In addition to promoting adult education and establishing adult remedial classes, they have also made great efforts to focus on vocational training for women, enriching vocational subjects, and hiring Ying Jianfu, manager of the Shanghai Bank Ximen Branch, to teach banking application, Yang Bingxun, a Master of Arts from the University of Kansas, to teach stenography, and Yu Binqi, director and technician of the Japanese Taisho Iron Works China Industrial Company Manufacturing Factory and inventor of the Chinese typewriter, and Ms. Jin Shuqing, a typing teacher from the former Nanjing Municipal Vocational Middle School, as instructors and typing teachers.

Ningbo Native Place Association Primary Schools: The Ningbo Native Place Association in Shanghai has established ten primary schools dedicated to enrolling children from their hometown. They are run with diligence, and recently the number of students has reached 3,000. The graduates from previous sessions have also made considerable contributions to society. The association, recognizing that many children from their hometown still wish to attend but are unable to, has decided to expand the enrollment of each primary school to meet their needs. In recent days, registration has been quite enthusiastic. It is reported that the first school on Qipu Road, the sixth school on Xinqiao Street, and the seventh school on Yangzhou Road still have vacancies.

Jingxiong Girls' School: Ji Xiazhong, principal of Jingxiong Girls' School in Xiehe Li, Parker Road, has decided to add classrooms and hire Ms. Zhu Rongxiu, a graduate of the Jiangsu Provincial Second Women's Normal School, and Cai Yingxiang, among others, as teachers to avoid the drawbacks of inadequate education due to overcrowding and to enroll a select number of students.

Kunfan Girls' Middle School: Since Kunfan Girls' Middle School at the intersection of Meibaike Road and Qingdao Road was approved and registered by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, in order to expand the enrollment of all grades in the middle school department, it has leased three adjacent buildings for expansion and has specially established a women's half-day remedial class to seek opportunities for women to study. It is now scheduled to hold new student admissions on January 27th.

Sports Circles Commemorate "January 28th" 154

All Chinese and Western Competitions Suspended Today

Today is the second anniversary of the "January 28th" Incident when the Japanese invaders attacked Shanghai. All Chinese and Western sports circles in this port have suspended work to show their deep condolences. Therefore, all Western League football matches, such as Donghua vs. Western Police, Youyou vs. Navy, and the matches of the Chinese Football Association and Shanghai Basketball Association, have been suspended.

Guangzhou Municipal Sports Association Rewards Private Construction of Sports Fields 155

(Guangzhou Letter) The Guangzhou Municipal Sports Association recently decided to reward private construction of sports fields to promote the development of sports. (Reason) The city's sports venues have always been insufficient. Therefore, the general public, except during their school days, rarely has the opportunity to participate in sports outside of school. In order to promote the universality of sports and strengthen the race, in addition to the government's efforts to increase the number of public sports venues, we should implement rewards for private construction of sports fields to meet the actual needs. Therefore, we have listed our humble opinions below for public consideration. (1) For private construction of sports fields that are leased for public use, all handling fees for construction procedures will be waived, and the Public Works Bureau will provide various construction conveniences. (2) For privately owned sports fields that are leased for public use, all taxes payable to the government, except land tax, such as house tax, police fees, and cleaning fees, must be waived to show preferential treatment. (3) When private land is converted into a sports field for public lease and there is a shortage of construction funds, the government will provide loans at the most favorable interest rate. (4) The rental method and amount of sports fields will be determined and issued by the Municipal Sports Committee for each field owner to follow.
