The Forward Line Takes the Offensive, But the Defense is in Danger 159

Lakes kicked off against the wind and advanced deep into the opponent's territory. Jinan issued a state of alert, and the surrounding defenders stood by with their weapons. Unable to Advance or Retreat, It is Repeatedly Breached 160

Jinan's five defenders worked hard and launched separate attacks, but things did not go as planned, and several attacks were unsuccessful. Ye Lunyan gave his life to protect the goal, turning around and deflecting the ball, causing it to bounce off his buttocks and into the net. After Lakes scored two goals, its momentum became even stronger. Jinan was under pressure and tried hard to resist, and managed to hold on for another ten minutes. Tuotuomen was active on the right flank, reaching the goal line and hooking the ball towards the center. Bao Shalie was prepared and succeeded with one kick, making the final score 5-0.

General Meeting of the Chinese Sports Association 171

Chu Minyi Presides Over the Adoption of the Constitution The Chinese Sports Association held its general meeting of members at its association headquarters on Dongxinqiao Street in the French Concession at 3 p.m. yesterday. Members Present: Those who attended the meeting yesterday afternoon included Chairman Chu Minyi, Directors Hu Puan (represented by Hu Daosheng), Wu Yunchu (represented by Liu Yunshu), Xu Zhiyi, Zhang Tianbai, Niu Tisheng (represented by Xu Xizhi), Xu Xizhi, Weng Guoxun, Xu Kaifu, Xu Guanqun, Liu Shaojun, Secretary-General Zhang Qidong, martial arts experts Xiao Geqing, Liu Wenyu, Zheng Huaixian, Hao Shaoru, Xiao Dequan, and more than 150 guests from all walks of life.

However, because there is no appropriate entertainment to pass the time, improper events occur during leisure time. Therefore, the best proper entertainment is sports. However, sports require a large sports field. However, Chinese martial arts can be practiced everywhere. Practicing them anytime and anywhere during leisure time every day will benefit both body and mind. As the saying goes, great achievements are embodied in a strong body. Only with a healthy body can we strengthen the country and the people. I hope that members of this association can popularize martial arts, recruit more members, and then martial arts can be promoted, he said.

Adoption of Resolutions: Subsequently, Secretary-General Zhang Qidong reported on the association's affairs and financial status since 1928, and reported on the newly hired Chairman Zhang Xiaolin, Vice Chairman Du Yuesheng, and others. Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Commemorating "January 28th" 172

— Ji Ping

Today is the "January 28th" anniversary. I think that not only the children of Shanghai deeply understand the significance of this anniversary, but even the children of the whole country are not confused about it! On this day two years ago, our great Shanghai suffered a fierce attack by the enemy. Fortunately, our army resisted bravely, otherwise Shanghai would have been in danger of being occupied!

The January 28th commemoration has passed twice. What is the significance of this annual commemoration? Everyone must think of some practical ways to reverse this catastrophe and wash away this stain of shame. Hey! Children! Middle-aged people and old people are probably not responsible. It is up to young and ambitious teenagers to work hard!

Think about it: Shanghai, known as the city of Eastern material civilization, is China's eastern gateway. If the enemy dares to attack from the east gate, can't we counterattack their west gate!

Children, remember, on January 28th, 1932, the enemy used airplanes and cannons to break through our east gate. In ten years, we will also use airplanes and cannons to demonstrate in the enemy's west gate. But one thing to note is that what we want to avenge is the real, ugly-faced enemy, not the unarmed, defenseless masses. (Because at that time, the enemy indiscriminately massacred our civilians, but we will never kill the innocent.)

Now is the world where the weak are prey to the strong. What "peace" and "justice" are all just deceptive fronts. If we continue to endure humiliation, then it will be difficult for China to survive in the future world. Children! This is a thorough statement from me. Remember Yue Wumu's Manjianghong:

"...With soaring ambition, I will feast on the flesh of the barbarian; while laughing and talking, I am thirsty to drink the blood of the Xiongnu. Do not idly let your youthful heads turn white, only to be filled with empty regret!"

I hope that the masters of the future will all be loyal and brave warriors who can emulate Yue Wumu's great spirit of "serving the country with utmost loyalty"!

Fighting the Cold 173

— Shi Yusheng

The northwest wind is howling, and the weather is cold, and the children are shrinking up.

The word "shrinking" is very appropriate. Look: lazy children, don't they just shrink at home and not go to school? Timid children, don't they just hunch their backs, shrink up in their sleeves?

Children, these are all unambitious and unprogressive kids. Today's China will no longer allow this kind of child!

What is there to be afraid of "cold"? Walk into the sports field, take a turn or two and run, kick a shuttlecock ten or eight times, and won't you be warm and sweaty? Hiding at home, shrinking your neck, isn't it just as cold? Moreover, the more you are afraid of the cold, the more you feel cold; the more you feel cold, the colder you get!

We ambitious and progressive children should not be afraid of the cold, but should fight the cold. Children, there are many things we need to fight for!

Candle 174

— Qiu

Tears welling up on the candle, don't be sad, don't be heartbroken, strive to fight for self-improvement, have a beginning and an end, and a sincere heart.

Magpie Cries 175

— Qiu

Magpie cries, guests are coming; Old bird cries, bad news is coming; I think magpies and old birds are both birds, all birds are good at crying, whether guests are coming or not, how would the magpie know? Bird cries bring bad news, superstition is even more ridiculous!

The Price of a Whistle 176

— Ms. Wang Wei

This is a story, very suitable for children.

When the late American President Benjamin Franklin was only seven years old, one day, school was out, and he filled his pocket with copper coins, preparing to buy some fun things.

He ran towards a store specializing in toys for children. On the way, he saw another child blowing a whistle, and the sound made him very happy. So, he gave all the copper coins in his pocket to the shopkeeper and bought one just like it. Franklin returned home, jumping and blowing the whistle, feeling very happy in his heart. The whole family was disturbed by the whistle. His older brothers and sisters knew that he had spent all his copper coins on just one whistle, and they laughed at him for being foolish, telling him that he had paid four times the original price of the whistle. If he had used the remaining copper coins to buy other things, he could have bought many more fun things.

They mocked him in this way. He felt very annoyed and burst into tears. This reaction gave him more sorrow than joy.

From then on, this incident became Franklin's motto. After he grew up, every time he saw someone buying unnecessary things; abandoning a stable life to pursue vanity; ruining their health to scheme for wealth; abandoning their future to seek pleasure; he would always say to himself: "Poor person, you have paid too high a price for this whistle!"

Finger Broken 177

— Bo Zhen

On the first day after the winter vacation, Cong'er had nothing to do. He suddenly remembered something that the teacher had told them to experiment with during the winter vacation. So, Cong'er quickly took a pair of glass cups, filling one with clear water, and a natural science textbook. Just as he was about to go to the study, his younger brother Min'er came in from outside and asked him in surprise, "Brother, what are you doing? Are you drinking cold water? The teacher once said, 'Cold water is not to be drunk because there are many microorganisms in it, and it will cause stomach pain.' Don't you know that?" The older brother didn't answer him and went to the study by himself with a loud noise. The younger brother was very strange and inexplicably followed his brother.

When they arrived at the study, Cong'er placed the cup of clear water on the desk, and at the same time looked through the book slightly, then he put the index finger of his right hand into the cup of clear water, looking from outside the cup, he saw that the index finger seemed to be broken. At the same time, a very happy look appeared on Cong'er's face because the result of his experiment was exactly the same as what was said in the book. But the younger Min'er was surprised because he saw his brother's finger broken, but he didn't feel any pain, on the contrary, he felt happy. He asked strangely: "Brother, your finger is broken, does it hurt?" The older brother smiled and said to him: "Brother, you are mistaken, my finger doesn't hurt at all. Because water has refractive properties, it looks like my finger is broken from outside the cup.

If you don't believe me, try it!" After saying that, Min'er still couldn't fully believe it. Hearing his brother tell him to try it, he put his finger in the water, and sure enough, he saw that his own finger was also broken, but it didn't hurt at all.

"What brother said! It's verified, I now believe that water has refractive properties." Min'er jumped out triumphantly.

Future Soldiers 178

— Jiang Gui Liang Zuo

The Myth of Snow 179

— Yin

The God of Winter brought the Snow Maiden. The Snow Maiden thought the world was too dirty, so she scattered snowflakes on the ground, turning it white. The children couldn't be happier, snow games: rolling snowballs, snowball fights, making snowmen... But, do the children know about a legend about snow? This is very meaningful.

Many years ago, snow also fell to the ground in winter; however, at that time, snow, like rice flour, could be used as food. Moreover, people at that time did not know how to grow rice and wheat; they used snow as their main food. They ate fruits in summer, and snow in winter. When snow fell from the sky in winter, piling up on the ground and in front of every family's door, people thought it would never run out, so they looked down on it. They didn't take it to heart, so they discarded the leftover snow, and didn't think about storing it. Instead, they trampled on it and insulted it.

Soon, the God of Winter knew about this, and he was very angry. He resented people for wasting God's gifts, and shouldn't have squandered food in this way. He made the snow turn into water when it encountered heat, and snow could no longer be used as food. He said to the people: "From now on, you will have to use your own strength to earn food." Although people were very remorseful, it was their own fault, and they had to think of other ways to earn food. So they invented cultivating grains to replace snow as food.

Reading Problems 180

— Da Zhai

Children, most of you are day students at school. When you return home after school, your parents are either working or taking care of household chores, and they don't have time to supervise your studies. But you must not just focus on playing. You must allocate a certain amount of time each day to review the lessons of the day.

In addition to reviewing, you should also buy some supplementary readers to read on your own. American elementary school students read several times more supplementary readers than textbooks, which shows that relying solely on textbooks is not enough.

I have seen many children who, after school, like to spend money at roadside book stalls to rent small stone-printed books, picture books, and novels. These books are absurd and superstitious. Reading them is harmful and not beneficial, and it is not as beneficial as reading supplementary readers.

There are many types of supplementary readers, including story books, joke books, and science knowledge books. If you look at the catalog of "Children's Books" in major bookstores, you will know what the titles of those books are.

When buying supplementary readers, you should choose ones that suit your level. There are ones for older grades and ones for lower grades. If you buy ones that match your grade level, you will naturally find them interesting.

When reading supplementary readers, don't flip through them randomly. You should read one book from beginning to end before reading another one. If there are any words you don't understand, you can ask your teacher or your parents. If you find it interesting, I guarantee you will enjoy reading it, which is much better than playing aimlessly.

A Word to the Mothers of Children 181

— Xi Shi

When I was young, sitting on my mother's lap, seeing the needle and thread in her hands, I always wanted to ask what it was made of, why it had to be so long, and my inquisitive mouth would never stop. My mother would get impatient and say, "Why are you always digging to the root!" Sometimes she was making my clothes, and I would always touch this and fiddle with that. My mother would get impatient again and say, "Why are you always messing around?" Children, do you understand what this means? I'm afraid many of you still don't understand!

An apple falling from a tree is nothing strange, but Newton saw it and felt that there must be a reason for it. He used the spirit of digging to the root to study it, and the law of gravity was invented by Newton.

What kind of medicine, what kind of glass tube head, we never like to play with it, and Edison, who sold newspapers on the train when he was young, he was a messer, an unprecedented great inventor, besides him, who else has there been?

Virtuous mothers, you should know that these two phrases "digging to the root" and "messing around" are not what you should scold, at the same time, our country needs countless children who dig to the root and mess around, because the interest and attitude of this kind of research in science and experimentation in science are born from these two phrases.

Correspondence with Rural Little Friends 182

— Zi Ming

Plum Blossom

Dear Little Friends: The wheel of nature, rotating to this point—everything shows desolation, sadness, bleakness, dimness, "nature" is like this, and "human affairs" are also like this. Especially

The current China! Little friends! Recognizing this environment is precisely the time when we cannot ignore striving for advancement—those who stand out in such an environment are considered outstanding, are considered my friends!

Look! The grass is yellow and the trees are withered, the flowers are gone and the leaves are faded. The grass and trees under the trampling of the God of Winter are not only "completely disfigured," but even their corpses are gone, who knows where? However, there are also strong-willed, patient and striving plants in the natural world. They stand greenly alone, shaking open their branches and leaves, proudly dancing and dancing in the wind. That is the pine, cypress, bamboo, and wintergreen plants. These plants are truly struggling out of the struggle! That is what is meant by "standing out from the crowd"!

Ah! There are also strange plants! That is the "plum blossom." At this time when the flowers are lonely, it insists on releasing fragrant blossoms. Its color, red and white, is beautiful without being gorgeous; its posture, scent... is completely "gentle and refined"! Many people have fallen under its branches, no wonder we want to call it the "national flower." This is truly the best of "standing out from the crowd"! Little friends, we would rather suffer our bodies and minds, use our wisdom, and be a person who "stands out from the crowd," rather than be greedy for temporary pleasure and be an "ordinary" child.

Right? No?

Fleas can jump a distance four hundred times their own length, and can jump to a height forty times their own height. According to this calculation, shouldn't a person of five feet five inches be able to jump over a place two hundred and twenty feet high in one leap?

Flies There is a kind of fly that can fly eight hundred and ten hours. Around the earth in seventeen hours. Compared with its record, what is the highest record of an airplane circling the earth?

Beetles can lift about three hundred times their own weight, while

Letter to Classmates Encouraging Them to Join the Boy Scouts 185

— Zhou Ling, Suzhou Jinghai Elementary School Student

Dear Sister So-and-So: Why don't you join the Boy Scouts that our school has organized? It's a lot of fun, so I'm here to encourage you to join. I wonder if you would be willing? Now let me tell you about the types and benefits of the Boy Scouts.

The Boy Scouts are divided into Cub Scouts, Boy Scouts, and Girl Scouts. Cub Scouts are organized by younger children, Boy Scouts are organized by boys, and Girl Scouts are organized by girls. You can join the Girl Scouts.

Although we have physical education classes, some things are not as thorough as the Boy Scouts. Physical education classes can certainly make our bodies stronger. But the Boy Scouts teach us the manners and morals we should have in all aspects, and can also make our bodies stronger. And it is of great importance to our lives, such as camping outdoors, not afraid of hunger, not afraid of cold, not afraid of wind, not afraid of rain, and you have to cook your own meals. If the clothes are torn, you have to mend them yourself, and you also have to save people, raise donations, etc. Everything must be self-governed and not dependent.

It is very important, if you develop the habit. It must be of great benefit to yourself. In addition to these beneficial things, there is also a very interesting thing, I think you will definitely like it, that is traveling abroad, wearing a uniform, without travel expenses, and people are very welcome, and you can also increase a lot of knowledge and knowledge, how happy.

We want to save the country, of course, there are many ways, but if we want to recover lost land in the future, we must start by being a Boy Scout from a young age, because we must have a healthy physique to bear the heavy responsibility of saving the country. Sister! Come and join us soon! I wish you academic progress!

Free Talk

"January 28th" Commemoration 186

— Hua Zi

Assuming I am a historian, and today I am writing about the "January 28th" Incident, then, how should I write to be considered "a direct account"?

In this anti-Japanese war, earlier opinions mostly attributed the credit to the 19th Route Army. However, as of today, the leaders of the 19th Route Army have become "rebels" and have failed. Therefore, some commentators believe that this is "self-destruction of history." Since the creators of history have already self-destructed their history, then the historian seems to be able to omit this entry.

However, it is not so. History is not something that can be arbitrarily added, deleted, or embellished. History is centered on facts. Objective historical facts are like iron castings, which cannot be changed. If the 19th Route Army did have anti-Japanese功, then this piece of history will be forever glorious. As for the later actions of its leaders, they are another kind of historical fact, which does not hinder the existence of the previous historical fact. History does not care about the merits and demerits of the characters, but only faithfully records each stage of the facts.

So, how should the historian write about the "January 28th" Incident?

"Shanghai People's Anti-Japanese War" - I think this should be the guiding principle.

Careful people may be able to see that this is actually a subtle way of writing, a bit like Han Yu's "Ping Huaixi Tablet," which obliterated the great achievements of the generals. But this view is wrong. Han Yu attributed the功 of 平淮西 not to Li Shuo but to Pei Du, and Pei and Li are two people, so the question of fairness arises. However, soldiers and the people can be regarded as one. No matter which army, when it is fighting for the interests of the people by the will of the people, it is the armed force of the people, and also a part of the people. Chinese soldiers have always been alienated from the people, and the people discriminate against soldiers. In the successive civil wars, only the people have been killed by the soldiers. Therefore, there is not only no connection between the "armed class" and the unarmed class, but they are also opposed to each other. In the "January 28th" campaign, the soldiers were 部in the position of the people, fighting against the enemy of the nation. According to the anti-Japanese generals of the day, "Shanghai's isolated army's ability to maintain the war for thirty days was of course due to the bravery of the soldiers, but the most important reason was the people's strength and economic assistance." This shows the importance of the people's mission in this war. Therefore, saying that the "January 28th" campaign was a "people's anti-Japanese war" not only points out its basic strength, but also points out the way for soldiers to make功. This is really the most direct account.

"China's war against imperialism must combine soldiers and the people." Although this is Chen Mingshu's words, it is also correct. However, from the standpoint of the people, it should be "soldiers must always become the armed forces of the people." "January 28th" did not leave us much. On the occasion of this second anniversary, what we consider most precious is still this lesson.

The End of a Famous Homicide Case in British History 187

— Lian Zhi

In 1483, a strange homicide case occurred in England: the twelve-year-old child emperor Edward V and his ten-year-old royal brother Duke of York, who were imprisoned in the Tower of London, suddenly disappeared. At first, everyone was baffled, but later they learned that the two princes had been murdered. This unprecedented murder case caused shock in the British government and the public.

For about two hundred years, everyone could not find the place where the two murdered children were buried. It was not until 1674, during the reign of Charles II, that workers repairing the Tower of London dug up a box under a staircase called the "White Tower," containing two sets of skeletons. The archaeologists at the time (we don't know what reasons they were based on.) thought that these were the remains of the two murdered princes. Charles II then moved it to Westminster Abbey and buried it next to the tomb of the British monarch. A Latin epitaph was also engraved, saying that the two princes were previously imprisoned in the Tower of London by his uncle Richard III, and later this cruel uncle ordered people to kill them.

Therefore, everyone agreed that Richard III was the mastermind behind this murder case.

In fact, people had suspected Richard for a long time. Thomas More, the author of Utopia, wrote an essay describing the process of this homicide case, and he insisted that Richard was the main culprit. Then Shakespeare wrote a famous historical drama called Richard III, and put the crime of murder on this British emperor. Later, this unprecedented tragedy gradually attracted the attention of the French. In the early 19th century, a French playwright named Casimir Delavigne imitated Shakespeare and wrote a very moving play called Edward. son of. Another contemporary French painter, Paul Delaroche, used the same subject matter to paint a profoundly moving masterpiece, which is now preserved in the Louvre Museum in Paris.

Among historians, there are also many people who agree with this hypothesis and believe that Richard III was the instigator of this murder case. They believe that only he could have done such a cruel thing. He had used swift means to end the life of his political enemy Hunstings; he had used a rogue priest to deny the formal marriage of his deceased brother; he had even slandered his mother in order to sit on the emperor's chair, saying that his two brothers were not born to his father. Such a cruel and immoral person, killing two nephews is naturally in his intention. But, soon some people came out to overturn this public case, to speak unjustly for Richard III, because ancient and modern historians like to do this kind of "overturning case articles" most. They said that the only historical data we have now for studying this case is that narrative written by More; but you must be careful! When this murder case happened, More himself was a three-year-old child, is the memory of old people reliable? And "孤證" is what historians are most afraid of because there is no way to distinguish its authenticity.

Playwrights and artists focus on character portrayal and disregard historical facts. Their words are even less reliable. According to these historians, this murder case was committed by Henry VII, three years later.

Therefore, this homicide case cannot be resolved. But this matter is no small matter, because it involves the reputation of the British emperor. The British government wanted to find out the truth, so in July last year, some workers were ordered to open the imperial tomb in Westminster Abbey and take out the remains of the two children for examination. The famous physiology professor William Wright, who is also the director of London Hospital, was entrusted by the government to take on this work. At a temporarily convened archaeological conference at the end of last year, Professor Wright gave a very detailed report on the results of his examination. He said that the two skeletons were indeed the remains of two children: one twelve years old and one ten years old. This is exactly the age when Edward V and his royal brother were killed. Richard's crime was thus cast like iron. Poor Henry VII suffered many years of injustice in vain!

We should pay attention: this historical problem. Historians themselves have no way to solve it, and as a result, they asked scientists to help. This shows the incompetence of modern history, maybe this is its progress.

Boring Text 188

— Ma Guoliang

It seems that when the editor ordered me to write an article, he told me to write something interesting. Therefore, when I picked up the pen, I felt a little 　　 in my heart. Humor is fundamentally not easy. There are always more ways to make a child cry than to make him laugh. There will never be people in the world who never sigh, but there are countless people who have never laughed. This shows the scarcity of humor and the difficulty of its creators. "Something interesting," what should I write?

For example, let's find some materials in the atmosphere of humor. But, in general, the atmosphere of humor, like movies, is talked about by people in newspapers every day, who is happy to read my non-movie expert's nonsense again. As for the hair of celebrities, the eyes of a certain Miss, the teeth and thighs of dancers, etc., people are talking about them in great detail every day. I really feel a little panicked that I have nothing to say.

Really, "something interesting," what should I write?

I don't often go to entertainment venues, and I don't have the ability of Mr. Lin Yutang and Mr. Lao She, etc., to write a crying matter into something that makes readers laugh, just like Chaplin makes the audience laugh. On the contrary, I often write a paper full of sighs about something interesting that people want to laugh at. You think, what else can I write?

It's not that there is sadness hidden in my heart, so I can't write interesting words with my hands. If I originally had the ability to write humorous words, then I might as well desperately hide the sadness in my heart and write the interesting words first. Just like what 朗却乃 said when he played the clown: "Smile, put on the mask of joy, don't let others know that you are worried." However, a person who can't say interesting words, even if he puts on a smiling face, is still stiff and can't evoke pleasure.

Forcing a smile is really not easy. In these days, anger is a crime, and even crying is not very free, only smiling, although whether the motive of smiling is automatic or not is another question. It's good for everyone to smile. Use a smiling tone to answer, and use the sound of laughter to decorate the walls of the hall. After eating, everyone should naturally laugh, hungry people, who shouldn't laugh too! Ding Guai Guai, on the night before he hanged himself, was still full of smiles and laughing at the audience, wasn't he? Whether smiling is easy or not, that doesn't matter, everyone should smile, but it is an ironclad truth.

Since everyone has to smile, then the person who is assigned to deal with the public must put on a smiling face and say something interesting to the audience. Unfortunately, I am one of those who have been dispatched.

I have no intention of complaining about our editor. He wants me to write something, of course, not because he wants to see it. He wants to show it to the readers. And he naturally knows very well what should be given to the readers. If it is clear that the public should be given cigarettes, but he gives each person a bowl of white rice, then it is really outrageous and unforgivable. So I don't blame him at all for insisting on asking me for cigarettes. But I really don't have any cigarettes on me, what can I do? I wanted to use vermicelli to deceive him into telling the readers that it was cigarettes, but I didn't have the guts. I can't stand the humiliation. The most embarrassing thing in the world is telling a joke and the audience doesn't laugh.

Nostalgia Sickness 189

— Hei Ying

Last night, I dreamt of returning to my hometown.

(Where is my home!)

Walking along a river, following the flow of the water. The water was yellow, carrying green leaves and coconut shells; flowing down, flowing down, the river water without end! But my home had arrived. It was in the place with the coconut tree, quietly, without the barking of dogs, without the crowing of chickens; only, the wind blowing the coconut tree leaves: such a familiar sound of my grandmother! I quickened my pace and walked over; the low attap house squatted under the tree, banana leaves like fans, half-covering the door. When I arrived at the door, I stopped, listening intently, but there was not a sound inside!

Where had they gone! There was my white-haired grandmother at home; and also my smiling mother, my innocent younger sister, all of whom I thought about day and night, didn't they often write to me asking me to return?

(Come back once! Grandmother is old, she is so eager to see you once!)

Quietly reciting the few words written on the letter in my heart; blaming myself for not returning until today. Now they all seem to have left home; my heart gradually became uneasy, and for a long time, I did not have the courage to raise my hand to knock on the door.

Finally, I forcefully pushed the door open.

Dark, damp, silent… “Mom”

The voice that called out obviously trembled severely. Calling out again and again, but there was no response. So I panicked, I ran to my mother's bedroom, the bed was still there, the table and chairs had not changed their positions. I turned to the kitchen, the stove was cold, the pot was left aside. In the living room, the large mirror reflected the dim sunlight, the calligraphy and paintings hanging on the wall were a little old; I saw myself in the mirror: my face was ashen, my thin neck and lost eyes were not how I looked when I was at home!

So I walked out again, I closed the door forcefully, forcing a bitter smile.

(If my mother saw me looking so thin…)

More than a year of wandering life had turned her son into what I am now; mother, how much your heart must ache! But what can be done?

The sky slowly darkened, and it was quiet all around. The wind blew with a bit of coldness, blowing past my ears, as if there was my mother's call; I couldn't help but shed tears.

(I woke up crying.)

Where is my home! Wiping away the tears from the corners of my eyes, I lay in bed, longing for my hometown.

My hometown is on Yidao Island.

But it is also in the southern country with the warm sun. I don't know if I should go back, a wanderer won't feel a sense of intimacy towards his hometown. But after having a hometown dream, I miss home: every day, I call out to my mother with the heart of a child, I pray for my grandmother's health. …

Father and Daughter (8) 190

— Jin Yi

"Thank you, I should go."

The female guest said as she stood up, looking around greedily once more, as if preparing to easily recall everything in her mind again in the future.

"You can sit for a while longer."

She also stood up, took down the coat, and helped the female guest put it on. When she approached the female guest's body, it was as if she smelled something, which made her feel so good. She could guess the reason, she knew that in order to keep life going smoothly, she could only say nothing.

She accompanied the female guest out of the house door, and was about to see her off, but was stopped by the guest.

"Don't come out, it's so cold outside, it's not good to catch a cold."

The female guest said this gently, giving her an instruction from a woman that she had never heard in her life. She obediently

replied:

"Okay, I'll listen to you, be careful on your way."

She stood at the door, watching the female guest walk down the steps, suddenly she wanted to run ahead and grab her clothes, and affectionately call out "Mom". She didn't know how happy that would make her, she had never called out "Mom" before. But she still stood there, with tears in her eyes, watching the female guest's blurry figure gradually disappear into the darkness. Her tears finally flowed down, she wiped them with her hand, turned around, and walked back to the empty hall.

She looked at the clock on the wall, knowing that her father would be home in fifteen minutes at most. She told the maid to tell the gatekeeper not to tell the master that a female guest had come to visit him.

The winter night grew deeper. (The End)

The Success or Failure of US Cotton Control is Uncertain 204

Managing Cotton Production... President Luo Expresses His Views

Reducing Cotton Fields... Some Show Opposition

A telegram from New York on the 16th reported on the cotton market in the past week, saying that the reaction in the cotton market last week was due to the management of the ginning case. The weather did not look good, and the reduction movement was also uncertain. At the same time, the gold price was also more stable. Southern spot goods were firm, and the supply was also thin. It is said that the Ministry of Agriculture is currently conveying to cotton farmers to let them decide whether there is an urgent need to force the management of production to prove the voluntary management procedures they have adopted. At the same time, the reduction of cotton fields this season is also in progress intermittently. However, there is a right-to-fear thing, that is, uncooperative cotton farmers will increase cotton fields to oppose the implementation of this plan, and the area is a total of 12 million acres. According to official claims, the contract is special 391,000 households, and voting has been held. As of January 22, the total number of joint operations was 1,712,000 bales. At the same time, 84,738 households had entrusted the sale of 299,000 bales. There were also 95,817 households representing 418,000 bales, which are still undecided.

Washington, 26th telegram, it is reported that when President Roosevelt read the issue of forced management of cotton production, his self-proclaimed best management method was to levy taxes when the number of cotton productions exceeded its quota.

There is a Changing Theory on Grain Loan Wheat Distribution

Standard Flour and Wheat Both Firm and Rising

Yesterday, in the flour market, after the opening in the morning, the prices for all months showed a firm and rising trend. As for foreign wheat quotations, Chicago was up by 2.00 jiao, and Canada was up by 1.00 jiao. As for the market situation, the current month's delivery is approaching, and both long and short positions inside and outside the industry must be gradually closed out. However, as the longs gradually have the intention to take delivery of goods, the position of the shorts gradually became unfavorable, and they frequently rushed to cover. Distant months were also good because there were rumors of changes in the government's wheat loans. The market sentiment was also good. When the market opened in the afternoon, the current month was steadily replenished by a small factory, and the longs refused to let go, so the market broke sharply. Distant months also entered a stable path due to the market sentiment turning firm. As a result, the current month rose by 2.25 fen compared to the previous day, February rose by 2 fen, March rose by 1.75 fen, April rose by 1.5 fen, May rose by 1.75 fen, and June rose by 1.25 fen. Yesterday, the wheat market was flat in the morning. In the afternoon, there was short covering, and foreign wheat quotations were good by 1, 2, and 3 jiao. Order placements have not been cost-effective for a long time, and there were also rumors of changes in the problem of wheat loans to factories. The market sentiment was upward, and short positions were covered. A certain factory purchased, and the prices for all months rose consistently, especially for the current month, because the spot wheat was scarce and expensive, and the replenishment was very heavy. The longs stopped returning, and the shorts did not dare to delay buying. Floating short positions were nervous and rushed to cover, and the price suddenly rose by 3 to 4 fen. The closing price was still strong, up 4 fen from the closing price of the previous day, 2 and 3 months were up by 2 fen each, and June was up by 1 fen. Spot wheat has been arriving in Shanghai in recent days. Yesterday, 1,600 bags of Shandong wheat opened at 4.18 yuan, Suqian wheat at 4.03 yuan, and Jiangyan wheat at 4.00 yuan, which was said to have been handled by Fuxin.

On "American-Style Compilation Methods" 233

— Fan

In recent years, a compilation method has become popular in Chinese cultural circles, known as "American-style compilation methods."

The spirit of this "American-style compilation method" lies in listing the opinions of various scholars on a particular subject, compiling them into a "new book" without criticism or conclusion. For example, when compiling or writing a book like "Introduction to Literature," if based on this "American-style compilation method," one simply needs to list the literary views of Hegel, Schopenhauer, Taine, Guyau, Ruskin, Dowden, Tolstoy, Plekhanov, Fritsche, Trotsky, etc.; as for the essence of their views, whether they are correct, one need not bother with them. This is the "American-style compilation method"!

On the surface, such a compilation method is indeed very "objective." It introduces the opinions of all scholars without criticism or conclusion, leaving everything to the reader's judgment. Isn't this "objective"? "Objective," yes, but here, it fully reveals the superficiality of those who compile or write books using this method; otherwise, it is their irresponsibility towards the truth. In fact, in every discipline, there are naturally many different opinions, but among them, there are both correct and erroneous ones. If one cannot distinguish between the erroneous and the correct, and simply lists them together in confusion, it shows that one's knowledge is too poor, and one is fundamentally unqualified to compile or write a book. If one can distinguish between the erroneous and the correct, but deliberately lists them together without criticism, confusing right and wrong, that is irresponsibility towards the truth! At the same time, in books compiled under such a compilation method, not only are truth and falsehood mixed together, full of contradictions, but truth can also become falsehood. Because truth is mixed with falsehood, it cannot clearly reveal itself, it is stained with the blemishes of falsehood, and the result is the same as falsehood.

However, this "American-style compilation method" has two advantages: first, it makes it very easy to compile a book, because it does not require much knowledge, just some reference materials, and copying down the views of various scholars will do; second, since it is necessary to list all kinds of views, whether correct or erroneous, the compiled book will certainly have many words, and therefore the royalties will be quite considerable!

However, one thing we should know is that the United States is a capitalist country where money is omnipotent, and this "American-style compilation method" is actually a compilation method under the domination of "money."

Hanging a Sign on Life 234

— Yun Fei

Due to financial difficulties, Su Fen was sent to a midwifery school by her father three years ago. In her father's opinion, although it costs some money now, after graduating in three years, it would certainly provide some help to the family's finances.

Su Fen finally lived in the midwifery school for three years. These three years have seen many changes: her father's death, the burden of tuition fees, the hardship of her mother and younger siblings' lives. All this has made Su Fen much more experienced in these three years.

Now that she has graduated, everything in the family rests on her shoulders. Her mother, younger siblings, and the family's livelihood all depend on her alone. What's most annoying is that she still has to repay many past debts.

Initially, she worked at the midwifery hospital affiliated with her alma mater. Because this was a kind of voluntary service, it was very hard. She had to work fifteen night shifts every month, and even during the day, she had to be diligent all day long. In a large ward, there were twenty or thirty lying-in women, but there were only two people on duty. The patients' requests for tea, water, food, and vegetables were really annoying. At the same time, she had to deliver babies in the delivery room. But she only received a stipend of fifteen yuan per month.

Therefore, for the sake of her family's livelihood, Su Fen resigned after serving for three months, intending to become a midwife on her own.

However, a difficult problem immediately arose: to be a midwife or a female obstetrician, one must hang a sign, and the home must also have considerable equipment, such as a telephone and a consulting room. Su Fen's family of seven was crowded into an upstairs room, with no telephone or consulting room, so hanging a sign naturally became a problem. Given her current situation, even if she got the landlord's permission to hang a sign on the door, it was unlikely that anyone would come looking for her.

To overcome this difficulty, Su Fen finally took a letter of introduction from her principal and went to XX Hospital to meet a certain hospital director.

"Ah! Principal Lu introduced Madam to practice medicine under a sign in our hospital. We are certainly very welcome. However, our place is very small, and the facilities are not very complete. I'm afraid it will greatly hinder Madam's business. It's best if Madam finds a better place!" the director said. After saying this, he revealed a careful smile.

Su Fen felt as if she had been splashed with a basin of cold water. However, she still mustered her last courage. She said: "Principal Lu entrusted me to convey to the director that she hopes the director can make special arrangements, because I really have no other choice now, so I came to find the director."

"Yes, but!" The director said hesitantly, "Okay! I'll be frank with you, because you are not an outsider. It's not impossible for us to support you, but our expenses here are very large. If you want to come and practice medicine under a sign, you must accept our conditions. First, you must come to the hospital at eight o'clock in the morning and return at eight o'clock in the afternoon. We will provide you with lunch. Third, two-fifths of your monthly income from deliveries should be used to help with the hospital's expenses, one-fifth should be used for food and advertising, and the remaining two-fifths are for yourself. Consider it yourself. If it's acceptable, that's naturally very good, otherwise we can't help. This is all entirely for Principal Lu's sake. Ha!"

A few days later, outside the gate of XX Hospital, a sign was added: "Female Obstetrician Zhu Su Fen."

She was indeed very busy in a month. Sometimes deliveries were in the middle of the night, and the cold wind was biting on the road. Su Fen thought of her [deceased] father and couldn't help but shed a few tears.

A month passed, two months passed. Every month, she could earn more than one hundred yuan by relying on the hospital's signboard. However, after giving three-fifths to the hospital, her own few tens of dollars still had to cover the expenses of rickshaw pullers, medicine fees, and maintaining the family's livelihood.

Time passed day by day, and Su Fen's life was still struggling and difficult. She often thought to herself: before, she was afraid of not having a job. After years of struggle, this is what it is now. What about the future...what about the future?

Women Use! Bamboo Shoot Husk Tubes to Collect Urine 235

— Li Dai

The coal mines of M Mountain in X Province are quite famous for their production. The coal mine workers of that mountain come from several sources: (1) Poor peasants or hired laborers who joined in order to earn a full meal; (2) It may sound somewhat like imagination, but it is true: some coal mine workers are single travelers who are suddenly kidnapped and sent there. The former do some short-term work, only carrying coal, so they are relatively free. The latter are completely slaves, with at most one meal to eat, and are kept in custody.

The workers in the pit are divided into two types: coal miners and coal carriers. The coal miners squat in the pit all day and night, chipping away, their bodies immersed in water saturated with various minerals, so at most, a person dies of skin rot in just two years. Due to incomplete equipment, coal is still carried out by people. The coal carriers carry a large basket of coal on their backs, bending over and crawling out of the pit, so those coal carriers all become hunchbacks. If there is too much carbon dioxide in the pit, the lit lamp will burn the entire pit, and no one needs to worry about the people being burned to death. Even if they are not burned to death, they will tear open their own chests.

The workers outside the pit carry large baskets filled with more than two hundred pounds of coal on their backs, which are placed on their shoulders. Therefore, apart from someone helping you load or unload the coal, you have no way or right to loosen it at all. The coal has to be transported from the pit entrance to the wharf or warehouse. The carriers are driven like mules and horses, running back and forth, without any stop, and even urinating is not allowed. Therefore, many women who carry coal have to use bamboo shoot husk tubes to collect their urine. The foremen then take this opportunity to take great liberties, even raping them while they are standing.

Speaking of wages, the foremen report the weight at will. They report the weight just as the scale is about to be hung. For example, if there is an actual weight of one hundred pounds, they at most report sixty pounds. If someone has a slight relationship with them, they may politely report seventy pounds. After working all day, they get at most three or four hundred cash (in that province, one large ocean [dollar] can be exchanged for twenty-four or five thousand cash). Three or four hundred cash is not enough to buy anything, so the workers cannot help but live on credit.

The mine owners are very considerate in preparing for the workers. They open many stores selling daily necessities, and the things sold in the stores are three times more expensive than in other places (outside the mine). If you want to borrow money, you can also do so, and you don't need to pay it back. You just work, so the workers not only have to work forever, but they will never be able to pay off their debts.

From their appearance, they are wearing a thin layer of cloth, and their whole bodies are as black as coal. If we didn't hear them still able to speak like humans, we would simply regard them as another kind of animal.

How to Learn the National Language? 236

— Lü Jingming

Currently, there are many places to learn the national language, such as the Chinese Vocational Education Society's affiliated Chinese Vocational Supplementary School, the National Mandarin Promotion Association's affiliated Mandarin Training Institute, and the Mandarin class of the Jingwu Athletic Association's Cultural Affairs Department... all of these are options. This article is intended for young employees who do not have the opportunity to attend school for supplementary education, so it only describes self-study methods for learning without a teacher.

Of course, learning the national language starts with learning the national pronunciation, which is the phonetic symbols. There are a total of forty phonetic symbols, divided into three parts: one is the initial consonants, totaling twenty-four; one is the medial glides, totaling three; and one is the final vowels, totaling thirteen. The first step in learning is to clearly recognize and pronounce correctly the "shape" and "sound" of these symbols. It is best for learners to gather a few comrades, buy a set of national pronunciation records together, and listen carefully and read aloud multiple times according to the order of the symbols. In addition, you need to put in some handwriting practice. You must practice until you can read a certain sound as soon as you see a certain shape, and write a certain shape as soon as you hear a certain sound. Only then can you be considered proficient!

The second step is to understand the nature and function of the initial consonants, medial glides, and final vowels. However, it is enough to know how to use them; it is not necessary to know why. In other words, the goal is to be able to apply them. If you want to study the principles in detail, it cannot be done within a short period of time. Once you understand their nature and function, then proceed to learn pinyin. First, learn the two-part spelling method, then the three-part spelling method. There are several kinds of spelling methods, some take the initial consonant as the outline and the final vowel as the detail; some take the final vowel as the outline and the initial consonant as the detail; some take the initial consonant or final vowel as the outline and the medial glide as the detail; some take the medial glide as the outline and the initial consonant or final vowel as the detail. No matter what the method, no matter how the arrangement, you must practice fully. The third step is to practice the pronunciation of the four tones. The four tones are the high-level tone, the rising tone, the departing tone, and the entering tone. When reading words in the high-level tone, be very flat, very natural, and do not use any strength. When reading words in the rising tone, you must read them very loudly, as if you are drawing breath up from your dantian. When reading words in the departing tone, to put it simply, it is like drawing a circle, and you must make the tone turn a corner when reading. When reading words in the entering tone, you must use force to pause downwards. For this practice, you can buy a national pronunciation vocabulary and study it word by word. You must read each tone with extreme proficiency and special accuracy. When speaking, as long as you look at the symbols and dots next to the characters, you will be able to speak the national language with a very authentic accent. You must know that phonetic symbols can only represent the sound of the national language; the four tones can only represent the accent of the national language. Accurate sound and accurate accent make for pure national language.

The above three steps are the basic work for learning the national language. Once you get the hang of it, learning to speak will not be difficult. However, you must learn bit by bit to have a chance of success. The method: each character must be read accurately according to the phonetic symbols and the distinction between the four tones; each word must also be read accurately according to the phonetic symbols and the distinction between the four tones. Once you can read characters and words accurately, then proceed to practice sentences, then practice a section, then practice a paragraph, and then practice an article. When you can write an article, you must not only be able to read it accurately, naturally, and fluently, but also be able to show the emotions of urgency and intonation according to the meaning of the words. Only then can it be considered a great success. However, following this method, you must at least select and read twenty or so articles that are close to natural speech before you can speak freely on what you want to say!

If you can follow the above methods to learn the national language and carry it out earnestly and persistently, success can be guaranteed.

Occupational Anecdotes

Occupation and Learning 237

— Hua

When I was about to graduate from middle school in the county, I suddenly felt panicked about my future after graduation. The positions of teachers in primary schools were already full, and a large number of middle school students continued to flow from schools to society year after year, batch after batch. I felt quite panicked that I would not be able to compete for a position, and I would still have to be unemployed even after reading books. So, I asked my family to go to the provincial capital to attend high school. I thought that after graduating from high school, I would definitely be able to solve the problem of making a living and have a way out. So, I tried my best to find money from all directions, and as a result, I arrived in the provincial capital.

In the first year of high school, I didn't feel anything, just went to class and played around, but in the second year, my heart became restless and anxious again. The problem that I thought would not be a problem before was hanging in my heart again. There were tens of thousands of high school and university students in the provincial capital, and most of those classmates who graduated were wandering around, idle, and without jobs. What's more, the money spent on high school was even more than that spent on junior high school? My heart was very panicked day and night. Ah! It would be good to return from studying abroad outside the province. The qualifications would be even greater, and it would not be difficult to find a position. What's more, the market outside is large, and it would be best to find a job outside. Getting into a certain university outside the province would fully solve the problem of my future. So, I desperately squeezed my family, borrowed from relatives, and raised even more funds to pursue even greater visions. So, before graduating from high school, I came to Shanghai, and soon entered a university in Shanghai.

Now, I am about to graduate from university, and the aspirations I have been pursuing, the panic about impending unemployment that I felt in the county and the provincial capital, the dream that was driven forward by this panic, is now gradually disappearing before my eyes. The panic is more severe than before, the money is spent more than before, and the future is more uncertain than before, and there is no further pursuit that can be made, no greater fantasy to cover this empty and hopeless hole.

Where is the way out? I can't find you! I think there must be quite a few people who feel the same way as I do, right? "Where is the way out?" has become a common problem. At first, we pursued and searched forward step by step, and thus also carried more or less hope, but the more we pursued, the more disappointed we felt. At the same time, the conditions in society that are sufficient to solve this problem are even more lacking: on the one hand, accelerated manufacturing and production, and on the other hand, a continuous shrinking market. If society as a whole has no way out, how can individuals have a way out?

However, it cannot be said that pursuing in this way will completely become an empty illusion. Of course, there are many who stand from an individual standpoint and look at this problem with an individualistic perspective and feel hopeless, or become pessimistic and degenerate, or go against the tide and act perversely. However, there are also those who, through this pursuit, grasp the fundamental cause of this problem. As long as the root cause of making everyone have no way out and unable to make a living is unearthed, it is very possible to further find a way out from this. Only when society as a whole has a way out can individuals have a way out.

Amateur Sports

Jumping Rope 238

— Cheng Xiyuan

Now let me introduce a very simple and easy exercise, which everyone can do. This is nothing else but an extremely ordinary and childish game - jumping rope. In fact, jumping rope is a very good full-body exercise, and its effect is equivalent to running. The difference is that when running, the body is moving forward, while jumping rope keeps the body in place, but the movements of other parts are exactly the same.

As for why you have to use a rope, can't you just pretend? The reason is very simple: for any kind of exercise, the first thing you need is to develop an interest in it (jumping rope also has various skills that can spark interest). Only then will it be beneficial to your body and mind; otherwise, it is easy to become bored and unable to persist.

Now let me write down everything about jumping rope:

(1) Benefits - Jumping rope is one of the agility exercises. Those who are physically weak and not suitable for strenuous exercise can do this. It can generate a large amount of exercise in a short period of time, increase lung capacity, and promote the metabolism of various tissues.

(2) Interest - There are also various skills that can be changed: such as jumping with both feet together, jumping with both hands crossed, jumping with both feet open in front and back, running style (one step one jump), and jumping over the rope twice, jumping with the hand reversed, and other kinds.

(3) Time - Only a few minutes of spare time is enough (it should be absolutely forbidden after a full meal).

(4) Location - Only six feet of space is needed, indoors or outdoors (but it is not suitable in places with unclean air).

(5) Equipment - A rough rope of five feet (can be recycled), costing no more than five cents. (6) Convenience - It is simple to use, easy to set up, and can be carried around. One person can do it during exercise (such as wrestling, ball games, etc., which must be done by two or more people), and no one needs to guide it (such as martial arts, dance, etc., which need to be guided by someone).

(7) Competition - If there are two people, they can compete with each other to increase interest. For example, taking jumping to a thousand as full, whoever jumps full of this number first is the winner. If there are many people, they can be divided into groups A and B to compete against each other.

Note: The rope is best made of cotton yarn and white hemp. Hemp skin and coir are second best. Straw rope is not suitable. Sports equipment stores also sell them. Both ends have wooden handles. The length of the rope can be random. The decoration is exquisite, but the price is very expensive, about one yuan or more.

Outlying Postal Agencies

Feet Bigger Than Head, Chicken Feathers as a Quilt 239

— Lu Fuzeng

Beijing Correspondence

Speaking of Beijing, everyone knows that it is our historical ancient capital and the central place of politics and culture in the north. This place retains the legacy of our country's feudalism and the remnants of ancient Eastern culture. The gray streets, the low bungalows, the simple and straightforward customs and habits, and the simple and pure social order, all explain why this gray ancient capital is often praised by many people.

In this gray ancient capital, people of all kinds naturally live. Many dignitaries love the quiet simplicity of this environment, so many live leisurely lives. At the same time, many remnants of the past officialdom who have declined, and tens of thousands of poor people, are constantly struggling in this ancient capital.

The weather in Beijing is usually very cold. In the past few days, snowflakes have been flying everywhere. The lakes in Beihai, Zhongnanhai, Shichahai, and other places have already frozen into ice one or two feet thick. The cold wind挟带着snowflakes whizzed through this cold city. Beijing is really a world of ice and snow.

Naturally, there are roaring stoves burning in the houses of many modern ladies and young masters. Even though the cold outside is already below zero degrees, it has nothing to do with them. In such cold weather, they sometimes hide in coats or fox furs and go ice skating in Beihai or Zhongnanhai. In their hearts, they naturally think that they are fighting against the cold.

In fact, for them, this is a very fun game. The cold does not harm them in the slightest. The real people who are fighting against the cold are the tens of thousands of poor people.

Once winter arrives, it is the misfortune of the poor. Many people, because of their livelihood, cannot but struggle with the cold. Those who have jobs have to run outside all day long, and those who can stay at home may not be able to have a fire to keep warm. However, they also have to work hard to struggle for their livelihood. Some people, in order to get a little fire to keep warm, get up early in the morning and carry a basket to look for coal cinders in the garbage dump. They look for coal balls or coal chunks that have not been burned by other people in the charcoal ash, and take them home to frugally light a little stove fire. However, the coal poison of coal balls is very strong. People who have no money are naturally unwilling to open the windows to let the cold wind in, so they often die from coal poisoning because of this. In the past few days, Beijing newspapers have carried such incidents almost every day.

There are also some people who work on the ice every day. They dig the ice from Shichahai, Beihai, and other places to be buried in ice cellars. In order to resist the cold ice under their feet, they often wrap their feet with straw, wrapping them very large, with each pair of feet wrapped larger than their head. In addition, there are some homeless beggars and poor people who are naturally even more pitiful. Every year, I don't know how many freeze to death in the streets and alleys. However, they also have a way to struggle. Because in the slums of Beijing, there is a kind of poor people's inn. It only costs two or three cents to stay in this kind of inn for one night. This is a short, broken house with many wooden barrels arranged inside, like those used to hold foreign nails or cement. This is said to be used as a bed. People who stay in the inn first hand the money over to the boss, and then jump into the wooden barrel and squat. The boss then takes some broken cotton, chicken feathers, and paper scraps to fill the cracks in the wooden barrel, which is used as a quilt. Then, the people in the barrel can also use these chicken feathers and paper scraps to resist the cold all night.

The desire to survive drives many people to live continuously in hardship. In this Beijing, many people not only struggle on the hunger line for many years, but also have to run past this cold death line in winter.

Several Small Monographs on the Inside Story of the Contracting System 240

— Wang Ceming

(1) Direct Contracting System

The direct contracting system means that the more you do, the more you get paid; the less you do, the less you get paid. It is a direct relationship between the capital side and the labor side. In order to gain more profit and avoid workers being idle - that is, so-called skimming - the capital side, in the process of rationalizing and dividing labor in their industry, pre-stipulates the labor price for a certain amount of output, such as the weaving workshop, winding workshop, and packaging workshop of textile factories, with a price of XX cents per bolt of cloth, XX cents per cart of yarn, etc. The tin packaging workshop of cigarette factories stipulates XX cents per pack. In order to make a living, workers extend their working hours as much as possible. Concerns such as "excessive labor" and "damaging labor functions" disappear in the sea of suffering from hunger and cold. This system is more beneficial to the capital side than the ordinary labor system. Although the wages earned by workers (contract workers can earn an average of seven cents per day, while ordinary workers can earn an average of four to five cents per day) seem to be higher than those of ordinary workers, this is not an extra benefit for workers (contract workers), but the result of doubled labor. At the same time, on the capitalist's side, it reduces the cost of employing foremen and gains more surplus labor. This system is mostly implemented in textile factories, cigarette factories, silk weaving factories, rubber factories, and so on.

(2) Indirect Contracting System

(A) Daily Labor Contracting System - The wages for daily labor contracting are calculated on a daily basis. Workers do not see the capitalists; they only deal with the contractor. However, precisely because of this, their labor is even less valuable and they suffer even more than direct contract workers, because they are subjected to double exploitation! Moreover, there is no limit to working hours. They must completely obey the contractor's orders. When work is urgent, they may have to work twelve or even fifteen hours a day. Their wages are usually around three cents a day. Construction contracting is roughly two cents a day, with food provided but no vegetables. Other contract workers, such as those in lumber yards and docks, only get one string of cash per day. If they work under the so-called double contracting, it is even more unimaginable, because all the double and triple contractors want to take a cut!

(B) Annual Labor Contracting System - This contracting system is even more cruel and is mostly implemented in Japanese-owned yarn factories. These workers account for about 25% or more of the entire factory, and most of them are female workers. Wages are calculated by the number of years worked. It may scare you to hear that they are given ten yuan for every three years of work, and some even less, and there are "selling oneself" voluntary letters signed. As for working hours, there is naturally no standard. They are driven like slaves who have been sold.

The reason why so many workers can still be recruited with such low wages and such hard lives is that the contractors successfully used the slogan of "providing food and accommodation." But from this, we can also see the tragic situation of the general working masses who "only seek to fill their stomachs."

Then, what is the food and accommodation situation of these workers like? In the dormitories on the upper floors of Japanese yarn factories, more than thirty people live in one room. There is no light or air to speak of. Brown rice is used for cooking, and vegetable peel soup is not enough to distribute. For the two meals of porridge in the morning and evening, each person is only given a few slices of dried radish. This is the actual treatment that the workers receive. If they are sick, there is no good hope except to be treated in the factory and "leave it to fate," because the factory has a rule that they are not allowed to stop working unless they are so sick that they cannot get up.

Responding to the Times

Commemorating "January 28th" 241

— Lie Kun

The second anniversary of "January 28th" has arrived.

No matter how forgetful people are, they will never forget that tragic and heroic day. As soon as "January 28th" is mentioned, everyone will think of the brutal and barbaric attitude of Japanese imperialism, and the bloody lesson given to us by cannons and airplanes.

On this day two years ago, many of our compatriots were brutally massacred under bayonets and guns, and our heroic anti-Japanese soldiers were engaged in bloody warfare in a fiery mood.

"January 28th" is a tragic and heroic day, and it is also the day when our Chinese nation became alert!

Now, two years have passed, and what we see is still the change of territory and the intensification of the offensive. Puyi's proclamation as emperor, the alarm in Chahar East, and the massive dumping of Japanese goods, how shocking are all these recent events to our nerves!

With the urgency of the global peace situation in the Pacific, it further shows that the position we are in now is no less than today two years ago. Everywhere is a powder keg, and everywhere is an unexploded volcano.

Therefore, on this day, the second anniversary of "January 28th," thinking of our compatriots who were brutally massacred and our houses that were burned down, how angry and sad we should be!

However, anger is not enough, and sadness is only enough to show one's own weakness! At this time, it is neither the time for anger nor the time for sadness. It is the time to prepare practically to welcome the future!

People with blood and heat, prepare yourselves wholeheartedly!

Famous People's Speeches

Mr. Shen Yizhen's Speech on "Habits and Life" 242

— Notes by Zhou Jianwen

What is "life"? What is "habit"? Broadly speaking, "life" means living, and living requires life. We cannot say that clothes, tables, pens... have life, because they have no life. We can say that plants, dogs, and people have life, because they all have life. So, what is the difference between having life and not having life?

Tables cannot move automatically. If you leave them there, they will always be like that. They must be subjected to external forces to move. But we animals with life are different. We can spontaneously generate many activities. Activity is the expression of life. The so-called life is the sum of all the activities of a person living in the world.

Analyzing all the activities of life, there are only five kinds. The first is linguistic activity. Everyone has to speak. There is no one who does not speak in daily life. Speaking is a linguistic activity. This linguistic activity occupies a most important position in life. The second is civic activity. Broadly speaking, civic activity refers to all kinds of activities in community life. We cannot leave society and people, so we should pay attention to the conditions of social life. Narrowly speaking, civic activity refers to political activity. The people cannot but participate in politics. The third is occupational activity. Occupational activity occupies a very important part of life. The fourth is leisure activity. Leisure activity is the activity of recreation in times of leisure. Playing chess and watching movies all belong to this category. A person cannot work all day long without rest, but we must engage in proper and beneficial leisure activities after work. The fifth is health activity, which refers to activities that promote physical health. Without health activities, the body will weaken, and at the same time, it will affect the mental aspect. Health activities cannot but be paid special attention.

Secondly, I want to talk about what is called a habit. We can say that habits are mechanical movements. For example, we walk very freely, which has become a mechanical movement. This is a habit. When a child first learns to walk, an adult must help him practice slowly, and often suffers many pains and difficulties because of the joy of walking, and even often falls to the ground and cries incessantly. This is because walking has not yet become a mechanical movement. Now let me explain habits from a physiological point of view. We have a nervous system in our body. Before learning, it is as if the road in the nervous system has not yet been built. Later, we continue to interact with the environment and gain many experiences. These experiences create many neural pathways in the nervous system, like roads. At first, the resistance is very high and it takes a lot of time, but after a long time of practice, the resistance gradually decreases, and later it is almost unhindered and goes very quickly, which is how habits are formed. For example, when we ask "eight times eight" equals how much, we immediately answer "sixty-four." When children calculate, they must read it in their mouths, count with their fingers, and roll their eyes, because the roads in their nervous system have just been built, the resistance is greater, that is, habits have not yet been formed. There is also one thing we must understand, that is, when habits have not yet been formed, the brain must pay attention. Our brain is like the central government. The spinal cord is a lower-level agency, like a provincial government. After habits are formed, the spinal cord nerves will manage it on its behalf, and the brain does not need to worry about it.

Finally, let us combine the two parts of life and habits and talk about their relationship. Simply put, "99% of all activities in life are habitual movements." Everything from getting up in the morning to put on clothes, wash your face, brush your teeth, and take chopsticks to put food in your mouth when eating, and all the movements of talking and chatting are habits. As long as you carefully examine your activities from morning to night, you can understand that habits occupy a very important position in human life. Life is a synthesis of habits. Since habits are so important to life, then how should we form habits? I think the first thing is to have deep attention. For example, if you are now looking at me, listening to my words, and not making any sound in your mouth, this is attention. Attention is the function of the brain. The greater the attention, the easier it is to form habits. The second is to have sufficient practice. The formation of habits also requires long-term training and sufficient practice, because through practice, the resistance of neural pathways can gradually decrease, making movements mechanical. This can be proved by experiments. The third is to have persistent perseverance. If you do it for a while and then stop, it is a tiger's head and snake's tail, an action that has a beginning but no end. Mencius once said: "If a man has no constancy, he cannot be a wizard or a doctor." Therefore, we must have perseverance in doing things. In other words, we must have persistent perseverance.

The Scenery of Greater Shanghai

Scenery of the Bund 243

— Xiao Ruiying

The Bund

This is the largest port in East Asia, the gateway to a metropolis with a population of over three million. It is the skeleton of the capitalist world, cast in steel and iron, the solid foundation of modern civilization, solidified with blood and sweat!

Here, great behemoths are moored, like countless mountains—large-caliber heavy artillery, the highest-record seaplanes, with wireless radios towering on the ships. This wireless radio transmits the pulse of this metropolis to London, New York, Tokyo, and Paris.

Ships—like fruits displayed in a fruit store, the President, the Empress, and vessels of the Northern Seas, the Southern Seas, and the Yangtze… Large, small, ten, a hundred, a thousand.

The river water roars incessantly, the waves in the Huangpu River surge turbulently, like the anger of the crowd. The wind blows the national flags on the warships—British, American, Italian, French, Japanese. On the shore, towering buildings rise like cliffs. These are classical, modern, expressionist, cubist, spewing out countless vehicles and crowds. HSBC, Yokohama Specie Bank, Citibank, Banque de l'Indochine… These monsters, pressing down on the heads of our four hundred million people, are constantly laughing wildly, ferociously. Their huge mouths are constantly sucking the blood of our country, from the nearest places to the far east, south, north, and west.

Nine-story tops flicker with fire-like red advertisements, the vehicles on the Waibaidu Bridge vibrate, emitting the sound of steel bones. In the Bund Park, pairs of young men and women whisper sweet nothings, while singles play with their hats.

The traffic lights on the street command the city's journey, and the red-turbaned Indian holds supreme authority in his hand. He is the maintainer of urban order, he commands the tide of people and vehicles, directing them through Avenue Edward VII, Nanjing Road, and finally, across the Waibaidu Bridge, towards the heart of the city.

At the head of the Waibaidu Bridge, the embassies of various countries stand majestically. The flag of New Russia and the swastika flag of the German embassy vie for dominance. The distant whistle calls, it is a signal.

On the Waibaidu Bridge, constructed of steel, electric trams and cars speed by like lightning. Young masters and ladies have just emerged from the hotels, their minds still wandering with the embers of last night's revelry. Whiskey, Chartreuse, Craven A cigarettes, and 4711 eau de cologne. Tenderness, sweetness, igniting the wild flames of youth in their hearts. Kissing madly, embracing, in the cars.

On the boats emerging from the Suzhou Creek under the bridge, many simple people from the interior continuously arrive, with simple hearts. But how can these simple hearts withstand the storms of this ten-mile foreign concession?

The Bund! It is the tip of this ten-mile foreign concession!
